<p><b><a href="/wiki/September" title="September">September</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2009" title="2009">2009</a></b> was the ninth month of that common year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Tuesday" title="Tuesday">Tuesday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Wednesday" title="Wednesday">Wednesday</a> after 30 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_holidays">International holidays</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/September_2009&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: International holidays">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>(See <b>Holidays and observances,</b> on sidebar at right, below)</i></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/September_2009&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from September 2009.</i></p>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background-color:transparent">
<tr>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div id="2009_September_1"></div>
<div id="2009_September_01"></div>
<table class="vevent" style="width:100%; margin:7px 0px; padding:2px; background-color:white; border:1px #cef2e0 solid;">
<tr>
<td>
<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 1, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-01</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">European</a> leaders remember the victims of <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a> at ceremonies marking the start of the conflict 70 years ago. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0901/ww2.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8230678.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2009/09/01/poland-second-world-war090109.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.time.com/time/world/article/0,8599,1919803,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Time</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantoday.com/category/world/view/poland-marks-anniversary-of-wwii-beginning" rel="nofollow">(Japan Today)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> celebrates the 40th anniversary of the <a href="/wiki/Coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="Coup d'état">coup d'état</a> which brought him to power. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0901/libya.html#Scene_1" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>'s streets are decked with thousands of multicolored lights, and hundreds of Gaddafi portraits and placards paying tribute to the leader, with celebrations attended by <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">African</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arabia" title="Arabia">Arab</a> and <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin American</a> leaders but largely ignored by the West. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2009/09/01/83589.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
<li>Gaddafi is hailed as a knight of revolution as celebrations get underway in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/01/muammar-gaddafi-anniversary-celebrations" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Gaddafi dedicates the first mass performance of a week of celebration to his adopted daughter Hannah, who was killed in an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1986_Bombing_of_Libya" title="1986 Bombing of Libya">U.S. air raid on Tripoli in 1986</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/libya/6121837/Muammar-Gaddafi-hits-out-on-40th-anniversary-of-Libyan-coup.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Uruguay" title="List of Presidents of Uruguay">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Tabar%C3%A9_V%C3%A1zquez" title="Tabaré Vázquez">Tabaré Vázquez</a> of <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a> shuffles his cabinet, with <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Fern%C3%A1ndez_(Uruguayan_politician)" title="Gonzalo Fernández (Uruguayan politician)">Gonzalo Fernández</a>, drafter of all major legislation, moving from Foreign Affairs to Defence. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/01/surprise-move-president-vazquez-most-trusted-advisor-defence-minister" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/List_of_heavyweight_boxing_champions" title="List of heavyweight boxing champions">heavyweight world champion</a> <a href="/wiki/Boxing" title="Boxing">boxer</a> <a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">Muhammad Ali</a> visits the birthplace of his great-grandfather in <a href="/wiki/Ennis" title="Ennis">Ennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0901/alim.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8232367.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/sport/othersports/boxingandmma/6123430/Muhammad-Ali-touches-a-corner-of-Ireland-with-his-visit-to-Ennis.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/01/muhammad-ali-freedom-ennis-ireland" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Speaking in <a href="/wiki/Lima" title="Lima">Lima</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/El_Comercio_(Peru)" title="El Comercio (Peru)">El Comercio</a></i> in response to some ironic quotes by <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peruvian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Peru" title="List of Presidents of Peru">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Alan_Garc%C3%ADa" title="Alan García">Alan García</a>, <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> says his country will continue to export <a href="/wiki/Oil" title="Oil">oil</a> to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> because it is "in interest". <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/01/chavez-takes-time-to-reply-to-peruvian-president-garca-ironies" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fiji" title="Fiji">Fiji</a> is suspended from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>, only the second full suspension in the organization's history. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8231717.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/rest-of-world/Fiji-suspended-from-Commonwealth-over-failure-to-restore-democracy/articleshow/4961084.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alain_Robert" title="Alain Robert">Alain Robert</a> scales Tower Two of the <a href="/wiki/Petronas_Towers" title="Petronas Towers">Petronas Towers</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, using no safety equipment. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8231076.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/2009915262522767.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nst.com.my/Current_News/NST/articles/20090901161343/Article" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unemployment_rate" title="Unemployment rate">unemployment rate</a> across the <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">Eurozone</a> reaches a ten-year high of 9.5%. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/8231310.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Chile" title="Politics of Chile">government</a> sets aside 4 billion <a href="/wiki/Chilean_peso" title="Chilean peso">pesos</a> for the purchase of more fuel-efficient trucks for citizens through its “<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cambia_tu_Cami%C3%B3n" title="Cambia tu Camión">Cambia tu Camión</a>” (“Change your Truck”) program. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/01/chile-launches-trucks-scrappage-plan-to-boost-economy-and-fight-pollution" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> <a href="/wiki/Phase-out_of_incandescent_light_bulbs" title="Phase-out of incandescent light bulbs">bans the manufacture or import</a> of 100 watt <a href="/wiki/Incandescent_light_bulb" title="Incandescent light bulb">incandescent light bulbs</a>, beginning a phase-out in favour of energy-saving <a href="/wiki/Compact_fluorescent_lamp" title="Compact fluorescent lamp">compact fluorescent lamps</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/europe/8230961.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pakistani_Army" title="Pakistani Army">Pakistani Army</a> claims to have killed at least 20 suspected militants in clashes across north-west <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/8231106.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An outbreak of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Diarrhoea" title="Diarrhoea">diarrhoea</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orissa,_India" title="Orissa, India">Orissa</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, kills at least 26 people and hospitalises 237. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/8230960.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A ban on <a href="/wiki/Katana" title="Katana">samurai swords</a> comes into effect in <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> in an effort to reduce increasing crime rates. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0901/samurai.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ali_Ben_Bongo" title="Ali Ben Bongo">Ali Ben Bongo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Mamboundou" title="Pierre Mamboundou">Pierre Mamboundou</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Andre_Mba_Obame" title="Andre Mba Obame">Andre Mba Obame</a> each declare victory in the <a href="/wiki/Gabonese_presidential_election,_2009" title="Gabonese presidential election, 2009">Gabonese presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/2009-09-01-voa18.cfm" rel="nofollow">(<i>Voice of America</i>)</a></li>
<li>91 countries agree to the first ever global treaty focused specifically on the problem of <a href="/wiki/Illegal,_unreported_and_unregulated_fishing" title="Illegal, unreported and unregulated fishing">IUU fishing</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/01/fao1" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jozF6o3ZudxKjNHdVnaj8w7cOVHQD9AEO9Q82" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.un.org/apps/news/story.asp?NewsID=31908&amp;Cr=fao&amp;Cr1=fish" rel="nofollow">(UN News Centre)</a></li>
<li>Documents released by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_government" title="British government">British government</a> show that the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> gave in to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan" title="Libyan">Libyan</a> demands that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lockerbie_bomber" title="Lockerbie bomber">Lockerbie bomber</a> be eligible for transfer home to serve his sentence there. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/09/01/scotland.libya.lockerbie.documents/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/02/content_11980947.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lankan</a> journalist is jailed for 20 years on charges of "inciting racial hatred" and "supporting <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a>" for writing articles critical of the <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Politics of Sri Lanka">government's</a> military operations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/asia/sri-lanka-jails-journalist-who-criticised-war-policy-1779889.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemalan</a> court sentences <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Felipe_Cusanero&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Felipe Cusanero (page does not exist)">Felipe Cusanero</a>, an ex-paramilitary officer, to 150 years in prison for the forced disappearance of civilians in the 36-year <a href="/wiki/Guatemalan_Civil_War" title="Guatemalan Civil War">Guatemalan Civil War</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8231142.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.boston.com/news/world/latinamerica/articles/2009/09/01/guatemala_convicts_paramilitary_in_disappearances/?rss_id=Boston.com+--+Latest+news" rel="nofollow">(<i>Boston Globe</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0901/breaking61.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE5800F720090901?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A plane carrying <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South African</a> Deputy President <a href="/wiki/Kgalema_Motlanthe" title="Kgalema Motlanthe">Kgalema Motlanthe</a> back from an <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> summit in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> makes an emergency landing on an unlit runway in northern <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Congo</a> after missing a fuel stop. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=136&amp;art_id=nw20090901121411601C499396" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Diarrhea" title="Diarrhea">diarrhea</a> epidemic kills 34 people in <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> and infects more than 5,000, with 500 hospitalised in <a href="/wiki/Addis_Ababa" title="Addis Ababa">Addis Ababa</a> in one day alone. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090901085002930C470042" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saba" title="Saba">Saba</a> threatens to secede from the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Antilles" title="Netherlands Antilles">Netherlands Antilles</a> in a letter to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dutch_Prime_Minister" title="Dutch Prime Minister">Dutch Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jan_Peter_Balkenende" title="Jan Peter Balkenende">Jan Peter Balkenende</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nrc.nl/international/article2345809.ece/Saba_threatens_to_secede_from_Dutch_Antilles" rel="nofollow">(NRC Handelsblad)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 2, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-02</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_2&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_2&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_2&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/66th_Venice_International_Film_Festival" title="66th Venice International Film Festival">66th Venice International Film Festival</a> gets underway. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8235030.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A helicopter carrying <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh" title="Andhra Pradesh">Andhra Pradesh</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Chief_Ministers_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="List of Chief Ministers of Andhra Pradesh">Chief Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Y._S._Rajasekhara_Reddy" title="Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy">Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Andhra_Pradesh_helicopter_crash" title="2009 Andhra Pradesh helicopter crash">disappears</a> during a flight in southern <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.arabnews.com/?page=4&amp;section=0&amp;article=126022&amp;d=3&amp;m=9&amp;y=2009&amp;pix=world.jpg&amp;category=World" rel="nofollow">(ArabNews)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iolu_Abil" title="Iolu Abil">Iolu Abil</a> is elected the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Vanuatu" title="President of Vanuatu">President of Vanuatu</a> during the third round of the <a href="/wiki/Vanuatuan_presidential_election,_2009" title="Vanuatuan presidential election, 2009">Vanuatuan presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rnzi.com/pages/news.php?op=read&amp;id=48866" rel="nofollow">(RNZI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/02/content_11985384.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Greek Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Kostas_Karamanlis" title="Kostas Karamanlis">Kostas Karamanlis</a> announces that he is to ask the president to dissolve parliament and call <a href="/wiki/Greek_legislative_election,_2009" title="Greek legislative election, 2009">a general election</a> for October. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8234843.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charles_Gibson" title="Charles Gibson">Charles Gibson</a> announces he will step down as anchor of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_News_with_Charles_Gibson" title="World News with Charles Gibson">World News</a> and retire from <a href="/wiki/American_Broadcasting_Company" title="American Broadcasting Company">ABC</a> in January 2010. <a href="/wiki/Diane_Sawyer" title="Diane Sawyer">Diane Sawyer</a> will replace him at ABC World News. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/WN/story?id=8471429" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> energy company <a href="/wiki/BP" title="BP">BP</a> says it has drilled one of the deepest wells ever in the <a href="/wiki/Oil" title="Oil">oil</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gas" title="Gas">gas</a> industry as it made a "giant" discovery in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story//bp-says-its-made-a-giant-oil-discovery-2009-09-02" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li>A 7.3 magnitude <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Java_earthquake" title="2009 Java earthquake">earthquake</a> occurs on at 14:55 local time on the <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> island of <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a>, killing at least 32 people. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/ap/20090902/ap_on_re_as/as_indonesia_earthquake" rel="nofollow">(Yahoo News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2009/09/02/73-magnitude-jolts-w-java-may-lead-tsunami.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE5811ZL20090902" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gmail" title="Gmail">Gmail</a> service is hit by an outage affecting the "majority" of its 150 million users. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/technology/8232971.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chilean</a> judge issues arrest warrants for 129 people for allegedly helping to purge critics of the country's former ruler General <a href="/wiki/Augusto_Pinochet" title="Augusto Pinochet">Augusto Pinochet</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8232996.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bernama.com/bernama/v5/newsworld.php?id=437409" rel="nofollow">(Bernama)</a></li>
<li>Two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Car_bombs" title="Car bombs">car bombs</a> explode in <a href="/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">Athens</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thessaloniki" title="Thessaloniki">Salonika</a>, damaging the <a href="/wiki/Athens_Stock_Exchange" title="Athens Stock Exchange">Athens Stock Exchange</a> and lightly wounding one woman. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0902/greece.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE5810P620090902" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ana-mpa.gr/anaweb/user/showplain?maindoc=7915298&amp;maindocimg=7915119&amp;service=100" rel="nofollow">(Athens News Agency)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> court sentences four security force personnel to death by <a href="/wiki/Hanging" title="Hanging">hanging</a> for their parts in a <a href="/wiki/Bank_robbery" title="Bank robbery">bank robbery</a> which left eight security guards dead. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/8233282.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=105074&amp;sectionid=351020201" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> blast kills <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> deputy chief of intelligence Abdullah Laghmani. The blast shakes the city of <a href="/wiki/Mihtarlam" title="Mihtarlam">Mihtarlam</a>, 60 miles (100 kilometers) east of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a> in <a href="/wiki/Laghman_Province" title="Laghman Province">Laghman Province</a>; it kills several government officials and wounds several civilians. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory?id=8468948" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> journalists held by <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> for illegal entry admit to crossing the border but claim North Korean guards arrested them on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> side of the border and dragged them back into the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE5810J120090902" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Michael_Jackson" title="Death of Michael Jackson">death certificate</a> of <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop star</a> and entertainer <a href="/wiki/Michael_Jackson" title="Michael Jackson">Michael Jackson</a> is amended to reflect his cause of death as <a href="/wiki/Homicide" title="Homicide">homicide</a> via "<a href="/wiki/Injection_(medicine)" title="Injection (medicine)">injection</a> by another". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8233250.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ennama_Asfari&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ennama Asfari (page does not exist)">Ennama Asfari</a>, the co-president of a <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Committee_for_the_Respect_of_Freedoms&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Committee for the Respect of Freedoms (page does not exist)">Committee for the Respect of Freedoms</a> in <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a>, is jailed for four months for insulting a policeman. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090902085659311C971504" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_government_of_Burkina_Faso" title="List of heads of government of Burkina Faso">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Burkina_Faso" title="Burkina Faso">Burkina Faso</a> <a href="/wiki/Tertius_Zongo" title="Tertius Zongo">Tertius Zongo</a> confirms least three people were swept away by floods and thousands are left homeless in <a href="/wiki/Ouagadougou" title="Ouagadougou">Ouagadougou</a> and its suburbs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090902054303516C145166" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A woman kills a man by jumping on top of him in <a href="/wiki/Barcelona" title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=79&amp;art_id=nw20090902114210839C223625" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Sixteen <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalis</a> drown after being forced overboard into the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Aden" title="Gulf of Aden">Gulf of Aden</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090901222755513C439238" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> reverses a ruling which had banned <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muslims" title="Muslims">Muslims</a> from attending a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Black_Eyed_Peas" title="Black Eyed Peas">Black Eyed Peas</a> concert in <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8233634.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Two British boys planning to create a <a href="/wiki/List_of_events_named_massacres" title="List of events named massacres">massacre</a> in a high school in <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a> are on trial after wanting to emulate the <a href="/wiki/Columbine_High_School_massacre" title="Columbine High School massacre">Columbine High School massacre</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/england/manchester/8233964.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>A 3,700-year-old wall is discovered in east <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8235041.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/tech/science/discoveries/2009-09-02-isreal-archeology-fortification_N.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctv.ca/servlet/ArticleNews/story/CTVNews/20090902/archaeologists_jerusalem_090902/20090902?hub=SciTech" rel="nofollow">(CTV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/02/content_11985716.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miyuki_Hatoyama" title="Miyuki Hatoyama">Miyuki Hatoyama</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s new first lady, speaks of riding a <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_flying_object" title="Unidentified flying object">UFO</a> to <a href="/wiki/Venus" title="Venus">Venus</a>, calling it "a very beautiful place" and "really green". <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSTRE5812DV20090902" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 3, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-03</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_3&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_3&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_3&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chief_Minister_(India)" title="Chief Minister (India)">Chief Minister</a> of the Indian state of <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh" title="Andhra Pradesh">Andhra Pradesh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Y._S._Rajasekhara_Reddy" title="Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy">Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy</a> is confirmed dead when the wreckage of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Andhra_Pradesh_helicopter_crash" title="2009 Andhra Pradesh helicopter crash">the helicopter that crashed with him on-board</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> on Wednesday is located. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/8235115.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/asiapcf/09/03/india.politician/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/Politics/Nation/Andhra-Pradesh-CM-dead-in-chopper-crash-PMO-sources/articleshow/4966949.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Economic Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/news/262770_YSR-dies-in-helicopter-crash" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> ministerial appointments:
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_Consultative_Assembly_of_Iran" title="Islamic Consultative Assembly of Iran">Islamic Consultative Assembly of Iran</a> approves at least 18 ministers for the 21 available posts. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/03/content_11991257.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marzieh_Vahid_Dastjerdi" title="Marzieh Vahid Dastjerdi">Marzieh Vahid Dastjerdi</a> becomes the first woman minister since the 1979 <a href="/wiki/Iranian_Revolution" title="Iranian Revolution">Revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8235264.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Legislators vote overwhelmingly to ratify <a href="/wiki/Ahmad_Vahidi" title="Ahmad Vahidi">Ahmad Vahidi</a>, wanted by <a href="/wiki/Interpol" title="Interpol">Interpol</a> in connection with the 1994 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1994_AMIA_bombing" title="1994 AMIA bombing">Jewish centre bombing</a> in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>, as defence minister. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/20099381637872956.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/03/ahmad-vahidi-iran-defence-minister" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The death toll from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Java_earthquake" title="2009 Java earthquake">2009 Java earthquake</a> rises to at least 57. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8235100.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/20099325923404861.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabonese_presidential_election,_2009" title="Gabonese presidential election, 2009">Gabonese presidential election</a>
<ul>
<li>The results of <a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a>'s presidential election were delayed as backers of the main candidates waited outside the offices of the Electoral Commission. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/atmosphere-tense-as-gabon-election-results-delayed-20090903-f9aq.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Syndey Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ali_Bongo_Ondimba" title="Ali Bongo Ondimba">Ali Bongo</a>, son of recently deceased leader <a href="/wiki/Omar_Bongo" title="Omar Bongo">Omar Bongo</a>, is declared the winner with 41.73% of the vote. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090903135323683C894455" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8235875.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Opposition supporters attack a prison and the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> consulate in <a href="/wiki/Port-Gentil" title="Port-Gentil">Port-Gentil</a>, amid several disturbances in the city. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iqI5qKc1Q2V2ptEWB4Qw4QTTk4YA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Research indicates the <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Galaxy" title="Andromeda Galaxy">Andromeda Galaxy</a> appears to have expanded by digesting <a href="/wiki/Star" title="Star">stars</a> from other <a href="/wiki/Galaxy" title="Galaxy">galaxies</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/science/nature/8234898.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>'s opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a> lodges an appeal against her conviction for breaching the terms of her house arrest. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0903/burma.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB125196376381582563.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8235314.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/asia/153383/burma-suu-kyi-appeals-against-conviction" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop star</a> and entertainer <a href="/wiki/Michael_Jackson" title="Michael Jackson">Michael Jackson</a> was laid to rest at a private ceremony during a sunset service in a <a href="/wiki/Mausoleum" title="Mausoleum">mausoleum</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Forest_Lawn_Memorial_Park_(Glendale)" title="Forest Lawn Memorial Park (Glendale)">Forest Lawn Memorial Park</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">USA</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/michael-jacksons-final-send-off-20090903-f9dl.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Syndey Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/SHOWBIZ/Music/09/03/michael.jackson.funeral/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="State Food and Drug Administration">State Food and Drug Administration</a> grants approval to a homegrown <a href="/wiki/Swine_influenza" title="Swine influenza">swine flu</a> vaccine, which producer <a href="/wiki/Sinovac_Biotech" title="Sinovac Biotech">Sinovac Biotech</a> claims is effective after only one dose. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/03/content_11990303.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/china-approves-homegrown-swine-flu-vaccine-20090903-f9cr.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Syndey Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Fresh protests are reported in the province of <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a> in western <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, after a series of stabbings with <a href="/wiki/Hypodermic_needle" title="Hypodermic needle">hypodermic needles</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8235305.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/news/international/Protesters_demand_Xinjiang_leader_step_down.html?siteSect=143&amp;sid=11163961&amp;cKey=1251974270000&amp;ty=ti" rel="nofollow">(Swissinfo)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.people.com.cn/90001/90776/90882/6747798.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>People's Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/200993101354185321.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> experiences its warmest August on record amid soaring winter temperatures. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8235111.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_Russian_Federation" title="Supreme Court of the Russian Federation">Supreme Court</a> overturns a lower court ruling in the murder of journalist <a href="/wiki/Anna_Politkovskaya" title="Anna Politkovskaya">Anna Politkovskaya</a>, ordering several probes into her death to be merged into one. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/russia/20090903/156008948.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/09/03/russia.journalist.probe/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>11 people are shot dead and a bomb at a restaurant injures 27 amid unrest in <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> south. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/local/153404/motorcycle-bomb-injures-27-in-south" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/asia/ten-killed-in-series-of-attacks-in-southern-thailand-1781028.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greeks" title="Greeks">Greek</a> Prime Minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Costas_Karamanlis" title="Costas Karamanlis">Costas Karamanlis</a> launches a difficult election campaign after calling an early parliamentary vote for October 4 to seek a new mandate and deal with a sharp economic crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/idUKTRE58235O20090903" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea F.C.</a> are barred from purchasing players on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Transfer_(football)" title="Transfer (football)">transfer</a> until January 2011 by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> for inducing <a href="/wiki/Ga%C3%ABl_Kakuta" title="Gaël Kakuta">Gaël Kakuta</a> to illegally break his contract with <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">RC Lens</a> in <a href="/wiki/2007" title="2007">2007</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thesun.co.uk/sol/homepage/sport/football/2622461/John-Terry-is-shocked-by-Chelseas-transfer-ban.html" rel="nofollow">(The Sun)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.skysports.com/story/0,19528,11661_5535793,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Sky Sports)</a></li>

<ul>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> grants <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a> a <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a> 500 million loan, its first to the country in 10 years. <a class="external text" href="http://www1.herald.co.zw/inside.aspx?sectid=9574&amp;cat=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessday.co.za/articles/Content.aspx?id=80568" rel="nofollow">(<i>Business Day</i>)</a></li>
<li>Temperatures in the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a> are at their highest for 2000 years, according to a new study. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/earth/earthnews/6131513/Global-warming-has-reversed-2000-years-of-cooling-in-the-Arctic.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> eases more restrictions on <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, allowing unlimited family visits and telephone exchanges. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/04/us-lifts-restrictions-and-allows-unlimited-visits-to-relatives-in-cuba" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/POLITICS/09/04/cuba.sanctions/index.html?iref=mpstoryview" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/03/AR2009090303810.html?hpid=sec-world" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 5, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-05</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_5&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_5&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_5&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/G-20_major_economies" title="G-20 major economies">G-20</a> finance ministers outline plans for <a href="/wiki/Bank" title="Bank">banking</a> reform, including tougher regulation of financial institutions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/g20-outlines-tougher-bank-regulations-2009-09-05" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/marketsNews/idUSL566412820090905" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>At least 15 people, mostly <a href="/wiki/Bulgarians" title="Bulgarians">Bulgarians</a>, drown in <a href="/wiki/Lake_Ohrid" title="Lake Ohrid">Lake Ohrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Republic of Macedonia</a>, as a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Republic_of_Macedonia_boat_accident" title="2009 Republic of Macedonia boat accident">tourist boat sinks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mia.com.mk/default.aspx?vId=67285723&amp;lId=2" rel="nofollow">(MIA)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8239659.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.makfax.com.mk/en-Us/Details.aspx?itemID=8647" rel="nofollow">(Makfax)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party</a> Chief in <a href="/wiki/%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi" title="Ürümqi">Ürümqi</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, is removed from his post following <a href="/wiki/July_2009_%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi_riots#Long-term_aftermath" title="July 2009 Ürümqi riots">recent protests</a> over a series of stabbings with <a href="/wiki/Hypodermic_needle" title="Hypodermic needle">hypodermic needles</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/20099510166606363.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8239591.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/05/content_12001223.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Foreign_Affairs_and_Trade" title="Minister for Foreign Affairs and Trade">Minister for Foreign Affairs</a> <a href="/wiki/Miche%C3%A1l_Martin" title="Micheál Martin">Micheál Martin</a> travels to <a href="/wiki/Khartoum" title="Khartoum">Khartoum</a> for meetings with the <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> government over the <a href="/wiki/Kidnapping_of_Sharon_Commins_and_Hilda_Kawuki" title="Kidnapping of Sharon Commins and Hilda Kawuki">kidnapping of aid workers Sharon Commins and Hilda Kawuki</a> nine weeks ago. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0905/comminss.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>An oil deal and trade concerns with <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> were at one point considered as factors in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lockerbie_bomber" title="Lockerbie bomber">Lockerbie bomber</a>'s release, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> Justice Secretary <a href="/wiki/Jack_Straw" title="Jack Straw">Jack Straw</a> says in an interview. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/09/05/libya.megrahi.britain/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of people attend rival demonstrations for or against the policies of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> in Venezuela, <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>, <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> and in other Latin American capitals. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8240188.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8240228.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC video)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hqPLqxS_foiK3XKaov6bmLnjidKgD9AHF39O0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.eluniversal.com/2009/09/04/en_pol_esp_venezuelans-join-no_04A2701893.shtml" rel="nofollow">(<i>El Universal</i>)</a></li>
<li>Around 90 people are arrested in clashes between <a href="/wiki/Right-wing_politics" title="Right-wing politics">right wing</a> anti-<a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamic</a> groups and anti-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fascist" title="Fascist">Fascist</a> protesters in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham" title="Birmingham">Birmingham</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/england/west_midlands/8239818.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jXrkd5wTHAGG9dSErLnEhqOq8EIwD9AHPKVG0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/rightwing-demo-ends-in-violence-1782532.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Grenada" title="Grenada">Grenada</a> releases the last seven prisoners convicted in the murder of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grenadian_Prime_Minister" title="Grenadian Prime Minister">Grenadian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Maurice_Bishop" title="Maurice Bishop">Maurice Bishop</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Grenada" title="Invasion of Grenada">1983 coup</a>, including former deputy prime minister <a href="/wiki/Bernard_Coard" title="Bernard Coard">Bernard Coard</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20090906-last-1983-grenada-coup-prisoners-released" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_6&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_6&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kilkenny_GAA" title="Kilkenny GAA">Kilkenny</a> beat <a href="/wiki/Tipperary_GAA" title="Tipperary GAA">Tipperary</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2009_All-Ireland_Senior_Hurling_Championship_Final" title="2009 All-Ireland Senior Hurling Championship Final">2009 All-Ireland Senior Hurling Championship Final</a> to achieve a record-equalling fourth consecutive victory. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/gaa/championship/2009/0906/kilkenny_tipperary_.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/national-news/heroes-return-to-catcalls-of-gimme-five-1880548.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li>Hundreds of people are rescued and a further 88 are missing after a <a href="/wiki/SuperFerry_9" title="SuperFerry 9">ferry</a> sank off the coast of the southern <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/regions/view/20090906-223813/Tilting-ship-in-Zambo-sinks" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Inquirer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSMAN456276" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/06/content_12003038.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8240224.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A third day of clashes take place in <a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a>'s second largest city, <a href="/wiki/Port-Gentil" title="Port-Gentil">Port-Gentil</a>, over the disputed <a href="/wiki/Gabonese_presidential_election,_2009" title="Gabonese presidential election, 2009">presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSL6362961" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gae1gawFUqRm2WJMEOf2u3Q6mU3g" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li>Ten people are injured in an <a href="/wiki/Acid_throwing" title="Acid throwing">acid attack</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rthk.org.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/news.htm?hightlight&amp;20090907&amp;56&amp;610244" rel="nofollow">(RTHK)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hikHmIcsFQBIw5XM43Wly5Eo0kqA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> orders a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> official from <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> to leave after he made "adverse remarks" to the foreign media regarding the <a href="/wiki/Liberation_Tigers_of_Tamil_Eelam" title="Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam">LTTE</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/asia/article6824039.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/south-asia/UN-officials-visa-cancelled-for-propaganda-support-to-LTTE-Lanka/articleshow/4980163.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.island.lk/2009/09/07/news3.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Island</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 7, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-07</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_7&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_7&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_7&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> asks <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> to explain a sudden discharge of <a href="/wiki/Dam" title="Dam">dam</a> water which left six people dead or missing across the border. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/07/content_12010187.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/northkorea/2009/09/07/15/0401000000AEN20090907005500315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20090907/156047157.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister</a>-elect <a href="/wiki/Yukio_Hatoyama" title="Yukio Hatoyama">Yukio Hatoyama</a> proposes a 25% cut in <a href="/wiki/Greenhouse_gas" title="Greenhouse gas">greenhouse gas</a> emissions by 2020, up from 8% by the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">outgoing administration</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantoday.com/category/politics/view/hatoyama-reiterates-goal-of-25-emission-cuts-by-2020" rel="nofollow">(Japan Today)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/20099771059232213.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/sci/tech/8241016.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Drivers in <a href="/wiki/Samoa" title="Samoa">Samoa</a> prepare to switch from driving on the <a href="/wiki/Right-_and_left-hand_traffic" title="Right- and left-hand traffic">right hand side of the road to the left</a> as a new law comes into effect, the first nation to change sides in 40 years. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8240992.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/lifestyleMolt/idUSTRE5861QV20090907" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gHv9dCCKAr79WLVGpt2eyB2NJoFQD9AIDGM00" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> formally approves the construction of new settlements in the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/meast/09/07/israel.settlements.barak.construction/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/servlet/Satellite?cid=1251804504656&amp;pagename=JPost%2FJPArticle%2FShowFull" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Central_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Central Bureau of Investigation">Central Bureau of Investigation</a> is to investigate the <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">helicopter</a> crash which killed the Chief Minister of <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh" title="Andhra Pradesh">Andhra Pradesh</a> <a href="/wiki/Y._S._Rajasekhara_Reddy" title="Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy">Y. S. Rajasekhara Reddy</a> and four others. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/india/CBI-to-probe-YSR-helicopter-crash/articleshow/4981749.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>Scientists working in <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">Papua New Guinea</a> announce the discovery of over forty new species, including a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bosavi_Woolly_Rat" title="Bosavi Woolly Rat">giant rat</a> weighing approximately 1.5kg. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/earth/hi/earth_news/newsid_8210000/8210394.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kraft_Foods_Inc." title="Kraft Foods Inc.">Kraft Foods Inc.</a> says it will pursue a takeover of <a href="/wiki/Cadbury" title="Cadbury">Cadbury</a> after the British maker of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trident_gum" title="Trident gum">Trident gum</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dairy_Milk" title="Dairy Milk">Dairy Milk</a> rejected a $16.7 billion bid. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601087&amp;sid=atVk42eW3GqY" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Premier of the Republic of China">premier</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (<a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>), <a href="/wiki/Liu_Chao-shiuan" title="Liu Chao-shiuan">Liu Chao-shiuan</a>, and his <a href="/wiki/Executive_Yuan" title="Executive Yuan">cabinet</a> resign due to criticism and public anger over the slow handling of the disaster during <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Morakot" title="Typhoon Morakot">Typhoon Morakot</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alertnet.org/thenews/newsdesk/SP494665.htm" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> activist <a href="/wiki/Lubna_al-Hussein" title="Lubna al-Hussein">Lubna al-Hussein</a> is found guilty of breaching <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_Sudan#Islam_in_Sudanese_law" title="Religion in Sudan">Sudanese criminal law</a> by wearing trousers, but is fined instead of being sentenced to flogging due to international concern over the trial. She has stated she will not pay and instead face a month in jail. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8241894.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jAZW89qny-VUhcZoGjzigD5oegKwD9AIJOVO1" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Sierra_Leone_shipwreck" title="2009 Sierra Leone shipwreck">shipwreck</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a> leaves "scores" dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/11/world/africa/11leone.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8247287.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/sierraleone/6168747/Two-hundred-feared-dead-after-boat-capsizes-off-Sierra-Leone.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/200-missing-in-sierra-leone-boat-tragedy-20090911-fjpq.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Police in <a href="/wiki/Milwaukee" title="Milwaukee">Milwaukee</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USA" title="USA">USA</a>, arrest a man in suspicion of being the notorious <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Side_Strangler" title="North Side Strangler">North Side Strangler</a>, believed to have killed at least seven women between 1986 and 2007. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/32721705/ns/local_news-milwaukee_wi/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>A colossal <a href="/wiki/Statue" title="Statue">statue</a> of <a href="/wiki/Apollo" title="Apollo">Apollo</a> is discovered at a <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a> <a href="/wiki/World_Heritage_Site" title="World Heritage Site">World Heritage Site</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hierapolis" title="Hierapolis">Hierapolis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://dsc.discovery.com/news/2009/09/08/apollo-statue.html" rel="nofollow">(Discovery Channel)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norwegians</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joshua_French_and_Tjostolv_Moland" title="Joshua French and Tjostolv Moland">Joshua French</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joshua_French_and_Tjostolv_Moland" title="Joshua French and Tjostolv Moland">Tjostolv Moland</a>, on trial for alleged <a href="/wiki/Murder" title="Murder">murder</a> and <a href="/wiki/Espionage" title="Espionage">espionage</a>, are found guilty on both counts and sentenced to death by a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of Congo">Congolese</a> military tribunal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.norwaypost.no/content/view/22478/26/" rel="nofollow">(Norway Post)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mobile_network_operator" title="Mobile network operator">Mobile network operators</a> <a href="/wiki/T-Mobile" title="T-Mobile">T-Mobile</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orange_(telecommunications)" title="Orange (telecommunications)">Orange</a> agree to merge their <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> businesses. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/8243226.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">magnitude</a> 6.2 earthquake strikes northern <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/europe/8243148.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://earthquake.usgs.gov/eqcenter/recenteqsww/Quakes/us2009lgbw.php#details" rel="nofollow">(USGS)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.geotimes.ge/index.php?m=home&amp;newsid=18181" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Georgian Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>35 people are killed and 44 remain missing after an explosion in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal mine</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pingdingshan" title="Pingdingshan">Pingdingshan</a>, <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8243175.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2009-09/08/content_8666610.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/20099824332357821.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a> replaces almost all of its senior police officers after they were blamed for deaths during <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%932008_Kenyan_crisis" title="2007–2008 Kenyan crisis">post-election violence</a> in 2007 and 2008. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.co.ke/News/-/1056/654698/-/umsmbr/-/index.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Nation</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8244594.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> journalist <a href="/wiki/Lubna_al-Hussein" title="Lubna al-Hussein">Lubna al-Hussein</a> is freed from one day in jail after being prosecuted for wearing trousers – the fine was paid by the Journalist Union. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jAZW89qny-VUhcZoGjzigD5oegKwD9AJAJDO0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/200998152754685257.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A storm, with rain, hail and winds of over 60 mph kills at least 14 people in northern <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> and southern <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8245351.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_9&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">US</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Representative" title="United States Representative">Representative</a> <a href="/wiki/Joe_Wilson_(U.S._politician)" title="Joe Wilson (U.S. politician)">Joe Wilson</a> (<a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">R</a>-<a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">SC</a>) interrupts President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>'s health care speech to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congress</a> with an audible shout of "You lie!" <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/11/us/politics/11Wilson.html?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aerom%C3%A9xico_Flight_576" title="Aeroméxico Flight 576">Aeroméxico Flight 576</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Boeing_737" title="Boeing 737">Boeing 737</a> carrying 104 people, is hijacked shortly after take-off from <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Cancún">Cancún</a>, and forced to land at <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City_International_Airport" title="Mexico City International Airport">Mexico City International Airport</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8247472.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Istanbul_Flood" title="2009 Istanbul Flood">Floods</a> in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a>, the worst in 80 years, kill around 20 people and injure a further 20. <a class="external text" href="http://www.todayszaman.com/tz-web/detaylar.do?load=detay&amp;link=120671" rel="nofollow">(<i>Today's Zaman</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE5883I620090909" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_of_Japan" title="Democratic Party of Japan">Democratic Party of Japan</a> agrees to form a <a href="/wiki/Coalition" title="Coalition">coalition</a> with two other parties, the <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Social Democratic Party (Japan)">Social Democratic Party</a> and <a href="/wiki/People%27s_New_Party" title="People's New Party">People's New Party</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://mdn.mainichi.jp/mdnnews/news/20090909p2a00m0na015000c.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Mainichi Shimbun</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8245483.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/09/content_12021794.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> accuses <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> of deliberately releasing water from a <a href="/wiki/Dam" title="Dam">dam</a> across the <a href="/wiki/Korean_Demilitarized_Zone" title="Korean Demilitarized Zone">Korean Demilitarized Zone</a>, in which six people died. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/09/content_12023043.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/national/2009/09/09/40/0302000000AEN20090909008000315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gLbEZ4_yLz8WPYhom2CwwzKLGa2AD9AJMT1G1" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> authorities close the offices of opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karroubi" title="Mehdi Karroubi">Mehdi Karroubi</a>, confiscating material. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/20099942010748275.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=105637&amp;sectionid=351020101" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>A new series of <a href="/wiki/Hypodermic_needle" title="Hypodermic needle">hypodermic needle</a> <a href="/wiki/July_2009_%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi_riots#Later_riots" title="July 2009 Ürümqi riots">stabbings</a> occur in <a href="/wiki/%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi" title="Ürümqi">Ürümqi</a>, northwestern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2009-09/09/content_8669084.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/news/272336_More-needle-attacks-in-tense-China-city--media" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=105738&amp;sectionid=351020404" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_427501.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The son of former <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Philippines" title="President of the Philippines">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Corazon_Aquino" title="Corazon Aquino">Corazon Aquino</a>, <a href="/wiki/Benigno_Aquino_III" title="Benigno Aquino III">Benigno Aquino III</a>, announces his intention to run for the presidency. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/nation/view/20090909-224337/Aquino-declares-presidential-bid" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Philippine Inquirier</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/asiapcf/09/09/philippines.aquino.candidacy/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,26050244-2703,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>North Korea holds celebrations to mark the 61st anniversary of its founding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2009/09/09/north-korea-anniversary009.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_427405.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stephen_Farrell_(journalist)" title="Stephen Farrell (journalist)">Stephen Farrell</a>, a journalist with <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i>, is rescued in northern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> after four days as a captive of the <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a>, but his Afghan colleague Mohammad Sultan Munadi is shot dead during the raid. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0909/breaking20.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>"Beatles Day" is celebrated worldwide as remastered versions of <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">The Beatles</a>' <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles_discography" title="The Beatles discography">albums</a> are released, as well as <i><a href="/wiki/The_Beatles:_Rock_Band" title="The Beatles: Rock Band">The Beatles: Rock Band</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsday.com/news/world/beatlemania-back-as-britain-celebrates-b-day-1.1432598" rel="nofollow">(<i>Newsday</i>)</a></li>
<li>"Cirno day" is celebrated, due to the date being ⑨.⑨.200⑨, by Touhou Project fans. The day was also called "The strongest day".</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_10&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
