<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a> apologises for the post-war treatment of celebrated <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">WWII</a> code-breaker <a href="/wiki/Alan_Turing" title="Alan Turing">Alan Turing</a>, who was chemically <a href="/wiki/Castration" title="Castration">castrated</a> for having <a href="/wiki/Homosexuality" title="Homosexuality">homosexual</a> relations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.number10.gov.uk/Page20571" rel="nofollow">(Downing St)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/technology/story/2009/09/11/brown-turing-apology011.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/entertainmentNews/idINIndia-42388920090911" rel="nofollow">(Reuters India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/11/world/europe/11briefs-turingbrf.html?_r=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/6170089/Gordon-Brown-issues-posthumous-apology-to-Bletchley-Park-codebreaker.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> says he will demand a permanent place in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> Security Council for <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a> and compensation worth 777 trillion dollars for years of colonialism in <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a> later this month. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=85&amp;art_id=nw20090910122616406C949734" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> court convicts <a href="/wiki/Du_Jun" title="Du Jun">Du Jun</a>, a former senior banker at <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Stanley" title="Morgan Stanley">Morgan Stanley</a>, in the country's largest insider trading case. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8248274.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a> bars opposition leaders from leaving the country following recent riots over claims of fraud in the <a href="/wiki/Gabonese_presidential_election,_2009" title="Gabonese presidential election, 2009">2009 presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8247830.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dubai_Metro" title="Dubai Metro">Metro System</a>, the first mass transit system of the Arabian Peninsula, officially opens to the public as its first <a href="/wiki/Red_Line_(Dubai_Metro)" title="Red Line (Dubai Metro)">metro line</a> is partially operational. <a class="external text" href="http://www.albawaba.com/en/countries/UAE/253346" rel="nofollow">(Al Bawaba)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Lebanon" title="List of Prime Ministers of Lebanon">Prime Minister-designate</a> <a href="/wiki/Saad_Hariri" title="Saad Hariri">Saad Hariri</a> steps aside in <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8248662.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/11/content_12032090.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>At least five girls are killed and 30 other students injured in a stampede at a state-run school in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> capital, <a href="/wiki/New_Delhi" title="New Delhi">New Delhi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2009/09/10/2682571.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0910/india.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> President <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">recognizes</a> <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> during a visit to <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.eluniversal.com/2009/09/10/en_pol_esp_venezuela-recognizes_10A2723489.shtml" rel="nofollow">(<i>El Universal</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE58924U20090910" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> journalists express anger over the killing of local reporter <a href="/wiki/Sultan_Munadi" title="Sultan Munadi">Sultan Munadi</a> during a rescue operation that saved his colleague <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Farrell_(journalist)" title="Stephen Farrell (journalist)">Stephen Farrell</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0910/afghanistan.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> consul John Terry is murdered in <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">Jamaica</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jamaica-gleaner.com/gleaner/20090910/lead/lead6.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jamaica Gleaner</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/us_and_americas/article6829343.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times Online</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greek</a> militant group <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Struggle" title="Revolutionary Struggle">Revolutionary Struggle</a> threatens to attack the "golden boys" it blames for the economic crisis as it claims responsibility for the <a href="/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">Athens</a> stock market bombing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0910/greece.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany_women%27s_national_football_team" title="Germany women's national football team">Germany</a> beat <a href="/wiki/England_women%27s_national_football_team" title="England women's national football team">England</a> 6–2 in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Women%27s_Euro_2009" title="UEFA Women's Euro 2009">UEFA Women's Euro 2009</a> final, claiming their seventh <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Women%27s_Championship" title="UEFA Women's Championship">European title</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/women/8246204.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A boat with over 250 people on board capsizes in a storm off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>, killing at least 8. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/11/world/africa/11leone.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.sl/drwebsite/publish/article_200512949.shtml" rel="nofollow">(<i>Awareness Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/200999234320873972.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Supporters of the traditional <a href="/wiki/Kabaka_of_Buganda" title="Kabaka of Buganda">Kabaka of Buganda</a>, <a href="/wiki/Muwenda_Mutebi_II_of_Buganda" title="Muwenda Mutebi II of Buganda">Muwenda Mutebi II</a>, riot in the <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Ugandan</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Kampala" title="Kampala">Kampala</a> after a move by the government to prevent him from visiting a local area, resulting in several deaths. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8249693.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090910175518798C143588" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=105870&amp;sectionid=351020506" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 11, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-11</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_11&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_11&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_11&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The search and rescue effort following the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Sierra_Leone_shipwreck" title="2009 Sierra Leone shipwreck">2009 Sierra Leone shipwreck</a> comes to end, with 90 confirmed dead and at least 100 others declared missing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSLB138950" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>In an interview with <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Libertas.eu" title="Libertas.eu">Libertas</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Declan_Ganley" title="Declan Ganley">Declan Ganley</a> says the <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">second Irish referendum</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> is "profoundly undemocratic". <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0911/eulisbon.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taiwanese_President" title="Taiwanese President">Taiwanese President</a> <a href="/wiki/Chen_Shui-bian" title="Chen Shui-bian">Chen Shui-bian</a> and his wife, <a href="/wiki/Wu_Shu-chen" title="Wu Shu-chen">Wu Shu-chen</a>, are both sentenced to life in prison after being found guilty of <a href="/wiki/Political_corruption" title="Political corruption">corruption</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.etaiwannews.com/etn/news_content.php?id=1054680&amp;lang=eng_news&amp;cate_img=83.jpg&amp;cate_rss=news_Politics_TAIWAN" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taiwan News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20090911-taiwan-former-president-chen-shui-bian-sentenced-life-imprisonment-corruption" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Zimbabwe" title="President of Zimbabwe">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a> condemns "bloody whites" for meddling in his country's affairs, specifically perceived <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> interference. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=84&amp;art_id=nw20090911145854961C691271" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Moldova" title="President of Moldova">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Voronin" title="Vladimir Voronin">Vladimir Voronin</a> of <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a> resigns. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/11/content_12035212.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Croatia" title="Prime Minister of Croatia">Prime minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jadranka_Kosor" title="Jadranka Kosor">Jadranka Kosor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Slovenia" title="Prime Minister of Slovenia">PM</a> <a href="/wiki/Borut_Pahor" title="Borut Pahor">Borut Pahor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Slovenia" title="Slovenia">Slovenia</a> agree on an immediate end to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slovenia%27s_blockade_of_Croatia%27s_EU_accession" title="Slovenia's blockade of Croatia's EU accession">Slovenia's blockade of Croatia's EU accession</a> and further negotiation of the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Piran" title="Gulf of Piran">Gulf of Piran</a> border dispute between two countries. <a class="external text" href="http://www.delo.si/clanek/88028" rel="nofollow">(Delo)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,4678032,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2009/9/11/apworld/20090911204945&amp;sec=apworld" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Star</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenyan</a> magistrate sentences <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jon_Cardon_Wagner&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jon Cardon Wagner (page does not exist)">Jon Cardon Wagner</a>, an <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> who founded the popular chain of coffee shops, <a href="/wiki/Nairobi_Java_House" title="Nairobi Java House">Nairobi Java House</a>, to 15 years of imprisonment for the statutory rape of three teenage Kenyan girls. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090911145110570C453854" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_verified_oldest_people" title="List of the verified oldest people">oldest person in the world</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gertrude_Baines" title="Gertrude Baines">Gertrude Baines</a>, dies in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a> aged 115. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5iuPqRuHpLY2dDl1KLZB6irSiYAogD9AL6OG03" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0911/bainesg.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kidnapping_of_Sharon_Commins_and_Hilda_Kawuki" title="Kidnapping of Sharon Commins and Hilda Kawuki">Sharon Commins, an aid worker kidnapped</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Ugandan</a> colleague in <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, makes contact with her family in <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> for the first time in several weeks. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0911/comminss.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s Space Shuttle <i><a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">Discovery</a></i> lands at the <a href="/wiki/Edwards_Air_Force_Base" title="Edwards Air Force Base">Edwards Air Force Base</a> in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">USA</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/science/nature/8249687.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> announces the discovery of a vast gas field off the coast of his country, one of the world's largest finds. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8251981.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/12/repsol-makes-huge-natural-gas-discovery-offshore-venezuela" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 12, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-12</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_12&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_12&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_12&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

</table>
</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Police in the <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Antananarivo" title="Antananarivo">Antananarivo</a> disperse small groups of opposition supporters opposed to the administration of <a href="/wiki/Andry_Rajoelina" title="Andry Rajoelina">Andry Rajoelina</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=84&amp;art_id=nw20090912221849853C708654" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A 6.4 magnitude <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=2009_Venezuela_earthquake&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2009 Venezuela earthquake (page does not exist)">earthquake</a> occurs in <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>, injuring many people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailypress.com/news/world/sns-ap-lt-venezuela-earthquake,0,763955.story" rel="nofollow">(Daily Press)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Lebanon_(2009_film)" title="Lebanon (2009 film)">Lebanon</a></i> wins the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Lion" title="Golden Lion">Golden Lion</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Venice_Film_Festival" title="Venice Film Festival">Venice Film Festival</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSTRE58B1JM20090912" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/arts/2009/0912/venice.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">President</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Nobel_laureates" title="List of Nobel laureates">Nobel Laureate</a> <a href="/wiki/Shimon_Peres" title="Shimon Peres">Shimon Peres</a> is hospitalised after a collapse in <a href="/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0912/peress.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/2009912213131638763.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/hasen/spages/1114124.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSMAC273201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/12/AR2009091202028.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Sierra_Leone_shipwreck" title="2009 Sierra Leone shipwreck">2009 Sierra Leone shipwreck</a>:
<ul>
<li>120 of the dead are buried. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090912200226386C548048" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>30 more bodies are found. <a class="external text" href="http://www.etaiwannews.com/etn/news_content.php?id=1055149&amp;lang=eng_news" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taiwan News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Taoiseach" title="Taoiseach">Taoiseach</a> <a href="/wiki/Brian_Cowen" title="Brian Cowen">Brian Cowen</a> denies <a href="/wiki/Libertas.eu" title="Libertas.eu">Libertas</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Declan_Ganley" title="Declan Ganley">Declan Ganley</a>'s claim that the <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">second Irish referendum</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> is "profoundly undemocratic". <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0912/eulisbon.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Eight people are swept away by flash floods and a ninth is killed by lightning as more thunderstorms lash southwestern <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>. Five people are killed in storms in <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090912174208949C638886" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>At least 11 people die following two days of riots in <a href="/wiki/Kampala" title="Kampala">Kampala</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=136&amp;art_id=nw20090912172126763C597144" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>At least 7 die in several separate attacks and suicide bombings in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/North_Caucasus" title="North Caucasus">North Caucasus</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5h9OHz4nVWKKUjgrraAGSlhUXSaNQD9ALS0CG0" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>At least three people die and several others are injured in <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a> when angry demonstrators clash with riot police. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090912130557635C208110" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>10 <a href="/wiki/Andy_Warhol" title="Andy Warhol">Warhol</a> paintings dating from the late 1970s are stolen from the private collection of Richard Weisman in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">USA</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8251948.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0912/losangeles.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> official Peter Mackay is revealed to have been expelled from <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> for challenging <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Government of Sri Lanka">government</a> assertions at the end of the <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="Sri Lankan Civil War">civil war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/11/sri-lanka-tamil-tigers-un" rel="nofollow">(The Guardian)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_national_rugby_union_team" title="South Africa national rugby union team">South Africa</a> defeat <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_national_rugby_union_team" title="New Zealand national rugby union team">New Zealand</a> 32-29 to win the <a href="/wiki/2009_Tri_Nations_Series" title="2009 Tri Nations Series">2009 Tri Nations Series</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sport24.co.za/Content/Rugby/TriNations/355/1d18ea2b38834678a46a90adba75c67f/12-09-2009-11-16/Boks_are_Tri-Nations_champs" rel="nofollow">(Sport24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=6&amp;click_id=2200&amp;art_id=nw20090912113458955C800093" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guatemalan_Army" title="Guatemalan Army">Guatemalan Army</a> is accused of abducting over 300 children during the 1960–1996 <a href="/wiki/Guatemalan_Civil_War" title="Guatemalan Civil War">Civil War</a> and selling them for adoption. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/americas/09/12/guatemala.child.abduction/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSN10417054" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> says a consignment of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a>-made missiles with a 300km range are due to arrive in his country. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/12/russian-mid-range-missiles-300-km-for-venezuela-and-they-dont-fail" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0912/venezuela.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>President <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a> says <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>'s first high-level talks with top <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">EU</a> officials in seven years went well. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8251978.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> announces that it will assist <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> in the building of a nuclear energy program.<a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601086&amp;sid=aElQ3UEU9eYM(Bloomberg)" rel="nofollow">[1]</a></li>
<li>At least 19 people die and 80 are missing after a <a href="/wiki/Ferry" title="Ferry">ferry</a> sinks in the <a href="/wiki/Congo_River" title="Congo River">Congo River</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of Congo">Democratic Republic of Congo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5ilOfUMCLAw2AybjxfRqmOQJdqH1A" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kim_Clijsters" title="Kim Clijsters">Kim Clijsters</a> of <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Wozniacki" title="Caroline Wozniacki">Caroline Wozniacki</a> of <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a> to win the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_US_Open_-_Women%27s_Singles" title="2009 US Open - Women's Singles">2009 US Open Women's Singles</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://straightsets.blogs.nytimes.com/2009/09/13/live-analysis-womens-final/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cork_GAA" title="Cork GAA">Cork</a> beat <a href="/wiki/Kilkenny_GAA" title="Kilkenny GAA">Kilkenny</a> in the final of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/All-Ireland_Senior_Camogie_Championship_2009" title="All-Ireland Senior Camogie Championship 2009">All-Ireland Senior Camogie Championship 2009</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/gaa/championship/2009/0913/camogie.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Police arrest more than 550 people in connection with two days of riots in <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>'s capital <a href="/wiki/Kampala" title="Kampala">Kampala</a>, as the death toll rises to 14. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090913121045211C157541" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> heavily criticises the "rich countries", the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/G8" title="G8">G8</a> and other international bodies over the global economic crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/8253318.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>German <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">Chancellor</a> <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> appears with her main rival, <a href="/wiki/Frank-Walter_Steinmeier" title="Frank-Walter Steinmeier">Frank-Walter Steinmeier</a>, in a TV debate, two weeks ahead of an election. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8253115.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,4682781,00.html?maca=en-rss-en-ger-1023-rdf" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/13/angela-merkel-steinmeier-germany-election" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/world/154270/german-rivals-spar-but-no-killer-punch-in-tv-debate" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bankok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/news/world/AP/story/1231251.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Miami Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>'s veteran foreign minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prince_Saud_al-Faisal" title="Prince Saud al-Faisal">Prince Saud al-Faisal</a> undergoes successful spine surgery in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE58C0NO20090913" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>38 people are killed in a <a href="/wiki/2009_Taldykorgan_fire" title="2009 Taldykorgan fire">fire</a> at a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drug_abuse" title="Drug abuse">drug abuse</a> clinic in <a href="/wiki/Taldykorgan" title="Taldykorgan">Taldykorgan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kazakhstannews.net/story/542546" rel="nofollow">(Kazakhstan News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hrJljl18Zvn6do8KN-NfJpBHUNXQ" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/exsoviet/20090913/156110641.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=3&amp;art_id=nw20090913090501360C548940" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Hundreds of people protest in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> over alleged beatings of its journalists in mainland <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> covering <a href="/wiki/July_2009_%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi_riots" title="July 2009 Ürümqi riots">unrest</a> in <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rthk.org.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/news.htm?englishnews&amp;20090913&amp;56&amp;611853" rel="nofollow">(RTHK)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8253036.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_429235.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 6 people die in a fall down an elevator shaft of a skyscraper under construction in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8253148.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=3&amp;art_id=nw20090913133702125C523073" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/accidents/news/article.cfm?c_id=13&amp;objectid=10597157" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>4 people die and 3 are injured when a mud house collapses in floods at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lazaret" title="Lazaret">Lazaret</a>, a poor district of the <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Nigerien</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Niamey" title="Niamey">Niamey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090913083902364C616794" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Two of the so-called <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_Triangle" title="Bermuda Triangle">Bermuda Triangle</a>'s most mysterious disappearances in the late 1940s may have been solved. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/8248334.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Teeth and bones from a range of animals, including <a href="/wiki/Hyena" title="Hyena">hyenas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Deer" title="Deer">deer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rhinoceros" title="Rhinoceros">rhinos</a>, are discovered by <a href="/wiki/Archaeology" title="Archaeology">archaeologists</a> inside a cave in <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/england/devon/8253091.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norwegians</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_parliamentary_election,_2009" title="Norwegian parliamentary election, 2009">Norwegian parliamentary election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iDznnIBsnqH1KsFNFHQp2c3MEAdQ" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.norwaypost.no/content/view/22505/1/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Norway Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>'s political "trial of the century" into the <a href="/wiki/Clearstream" title="Clearstream">Clearstream</a> affair—former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Dominique_de_Villepin" title="Dominique de Villepin">Dominique de Villepin</a> versus <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a>—opens at the <a href="/wiki/Palais_de_Justice,_Paris" title="Palais de Justice, Paris">Palais de Justice</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/sarkozys-sexual-history-to-go-on-show-in-court-20090913-fm8p.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baraawe_Raid" title="Baraawe Raid">U.S. special forces launch an attack</a> on <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamist</a> militants from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(Somalia)" title="Al-Shabaab (Somalia)">Al-Shabab</a> in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8254957.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.mareeg.com/fidsan.php?sid=13696&amp;tirsan=3" rel="nofollow">(Mareeg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/reuters/2009/09/14/world/international-uk-somalia-conflict.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 18 women and children are killed in a stampede for free flour handed out by charity workers in <a href="/wiki/Karachi" title="Karachi">Karachi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2009/09/2009914121530382141.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.com.pk/pakistan-news-newspaper-daily-english-online/Karachi/14-Sep-2009/18-killed-several-injured-in-Karachi-stampede-police" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Nation</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/14/content_12051335.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Legislators in <a href="/wiki/Aceh" title="Aceh">Aceh</a> province in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> pass a new law on <a href="/wiki/Stoning" title="Stoning">stoning</a> to death and other severe sentences for <a href="/wiki/Adultery" title="Adultery">adultery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Homosexuality" title="Homosexuality">homosexuality</a> and <a href="/wiki/Premarital_sex" title="Premarital sex">premarital sex</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2009/09/14/indonesia039s-aceh-passes-law-stoning-death.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/200991418142587643.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/14/indonesia-aceh-adultery-stoning-death" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Dozens of people in <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a> are charged over riots in the capital <a href="/wiki/Kampala" title="Kampala">Kampala</a> over the visit of the <a href="/wiki/Kabaka_of_Buganda" title="Kabaka of Buganda">King of Buganda</a>, <a href="/wiki/Muwenda_Mutebi_II_of_Buganda" title="Muwenda Mutebi II of Buganda">Ronald Muwenda Mutebi II</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8254080.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> lodges a complaint with the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a> over the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>' decision to impose import duties on Chinese-made <a href="/wiki/Tire" title="Tire">tires</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2009-09/14/content_8690565.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/b5068b0e-a151-11de-a88d-00144feabdc0.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A large area of <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, is evacuated after a <a href="/wiki/Pipe_bomb" title="Pipe bomb">Pipe bomb</a> was found in a truck, but the bomb is neutralized by the <a href="/wiki/Toronto_Police_Service" title="Toronto Police Service">Toronto bomb squad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cp24.com/servlet/an/local/CTVNews/20090914/090914_evacuation/20090914/?hub=CP24Home" rel="nofollow">(CP24)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mart%C3%ADn_del_Potro" title="Juan Martín del Potro">Juan Martín del Potro</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Roger_Federer" title="Roger Federer">Roger Federer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kim_Clijsters" title="Kim Clijsters">Kim Clijsters</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Wozniacki" title="Caroline Wozniacki">Caroline Wozniacki</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Open_(tennis)" title="U.S. Open (tennis)">U.S. Open</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://straightsets.blogs.nytimes.com/2009/09/14/del-potro-stuns-federer-to-win-open/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Swayze" title="Patrick Swayze">Patrick Swayze</a> dies at age 57, after suffering from <a href="/wiki/Pancreatic_cancer" title="Pancreatic cancer">pancreatic cancer</a> for more than 1 year. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8256033.stm" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red-Green_Coalition_(Norway)" title="Red-Green Coalition (Norway)">Red-Green Coalition</a> of <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Norway" title="Prime Minister of Norway">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jens_Stoltenberg" title="Jens Stoltenberg">Jens Stoltenberg</a> is elected for another term in the <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norwegian</a> <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_parliamentary_election,_2009" title="Norwegian parliamentary election, 2009">parliamentary election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.norwaypost.no/content/view/22509/1/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Norway Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/58a1ac9e-a14d-11de-a88d-00144feabdc0.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 38 people are killed in flash floods in <a href="/wiki/North_Sumatra" title="North Sumatra">North Sumatra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0915/indonesia.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve" title="Federal Reserve">Federal Reserve</a> Chairman <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ben_S._Bernanke" title="Ben S. Bernanke">Ben S. Bernanke</a> says the worst <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S." title="U.S.">U.S.</a> recession since the 1930s has likely ended, while warning that growth may not be strong enough to quickly reduce the unemployment rate. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601087&amp;sid=aflWYD0hCPqA" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a> accuses the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> of "blocking" <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s accession to the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/09/15/russia.us.wto/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> report into the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_War_(2008%E2%80%9309)" title="Gaza War (2008–09)">Gaza War</a> alleges both <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> and <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestinian</a> forces committed <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/8257301.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2009/09/2009915142916822510.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/EirGrid" title="EirGrid">EirGrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s national electricity grid operator, receives permission from <a href="/wiki/An_Bord_Plean%C3%A1la" title="An Bord Pleanála">An Bord Pleanála</a> to build a new electricity interconnector between Ireland and <a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">Wales</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0915/electricity1.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabonese</a> firefighters battle a blaze at the heart of <a href="/wiki/Libreville" title="Libreville">Libreville</a> as fire consumes the nation's largest market. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=136&amp;art_id=nw20090916082550586C938366" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Republic of the Congo">Republic of the Congo</a>'s re-elected <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_the_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="List of heads of state of the Republic of the Congo">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Denis_Sassou_Nguesso" title="Denis Sassou Nguesso">Denis Sassou Nguesso</a> names his new government, abolishing the controversial post of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_government_of_the_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="List of heads of government of the Republic of the Congo">Prime Minister</a> and replacing the nation's oil minister. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=136&amp;art_id=nw20090916132725546C641341" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>In a televised debate, <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Madagascar" title="Prime Minister of Madagascar">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Monja_Roindefo" title="Monja Roindefo">Monja Roindefo</a> accuses the international community of betraying <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Madagascar" title="List of Presidents of Madagascar">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Andry_Rajoelina" title="Andry Rajoelina">Andry Rajoelina</a> and warns the island risks being "torn into <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fiefdom" title="Fiefdom">fiefdoms</a> ruled by <a href="/wiki/Warlord" title="Warlord">warlords</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=84&amp;art_id=nw20090916132627133C675798" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 16, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-16</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_16&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_16&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_16&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>New documents disclose that novelist <a href="/wiki/J._R._R._Tolkien" title="J. R. R. Tolkien">J. R. R. Tolkien</a> secretly trained as a spy for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Her_Majesty%27s_Government" title="Her Majesty's Government">His Majesty's Government</a> in the run up to <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/6197169/JRR-Tolkien-trained-as-British-spy.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Manuel_Barroso" title="José Manuel Barroso">José Manuel Barroso</a> is re-elected as <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_European_Commission" title="President of the European Commission">President of the European Commission</a>, by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Members_of_the_European_Parliament" title="Members of the European Parliament">Members of the European Parliament</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/europe/8258387.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.portalangop.co.ao/motix/en_us/noticias/internacional/2009/8/38/Euro-MPs-give-Barroso-new-mandate,59db8322-56da-4173-88ce-4107ef2c461b.html" rel="nofollow">(Angola Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yukio_Hatoyama" title="Yukio Hatoyama">Yukio Hatoyama</a> is sworn in as the 60th <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.asahi.com/english/Herald-asahi/TKY200909160216.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Asahi Shimbun</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.radioaustralia.net.au/asiapac/stories/200909/s2688162.htm" rel="nofollow">(Radio Australia)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> announces that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> is to invest 16 billion <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US dollars</a> to boost oil production in the country particularly along the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orinoco_River" title="Orinoco River">Orinoco River</a> as part of a strategy to reduce dependence on the US market. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/17/china-to-invest-16-billion-usd-to-develop-new-oilfields-in-venezuela" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> formally accepts apologies from the <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> government which admitted having committed a “protocol error” on allowing the presence of a delegation from the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> in an international fisheries sustainability conference. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/16/spanish-apology-to-argentina-for-protocol-error-involving-falklands-delegat" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>'s parliament nullifies <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Kenya" title="List of heads of state of Kenya">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mwai_Kibaki" title="Mwai Kibaki">Mwai Kibaki</a>'s reappointment of Kenya's anti-corruption chief, <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Ringera" title="Aaron Ringera">Justice Aaron Ringera</a>, who critics say has shown little interest in fighting graft. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090916223252835C819002" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> casts doubt on last month's election results showing <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> President <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a> winning the presidential election outright in the first round. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE58F1QJ20090916" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organisation" title="World Meteorological Organisation">World Meteorological Organisation</a> says the <a href="/wiki/Ozone_depletion" title="Ozone depletion">hole</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Ozone_layer" title="Ozone layer">Ozone layer</a> is smaller than in 2008. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5h4xfGKiBGIZBnS1nMb1PrKRhmgjA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> says it has foiled a possible terrorist attack in <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>, detaining six people. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/16/content_12063707.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_430651.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/2009/09/16/China-arrests-Uighur-terrorists/UPI-64291253119127/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalian</a> <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamist</a> group <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(Somalia)" title="Al-Shabaab (Somalia)">Al-Shabaab</a> call for reinforcements after a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> raid killed its leader <a href="/wiki/Saleh_Ali_Saleh_Nabhan" title="Saleh Ali Saleh Nabhan">Saleh Ali Saleh Nabhan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE58F4O820090916" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Gunmen kill 10 people at a drug rehabilitation clinic in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gMi5B2USfJStXxfqgWWr2xjRYpOgD9AOI5TG0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/americas/09/16/mexico.killings/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a> begins moving the first residents out of <a href="/wiki/Slum" title="Slum">slums</a> in the capital <a href="/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a>, as part of a plan to clear all <a href="/wiki/Shanty_town" title="Shanty town">shanty towns</a> over the next two to five years. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8258417.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5i2mIs1YGVZOqru3LLXpzLNtLJDnQD9AOF4C00" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.capitalfm.co.ke/news/Kenyanews/Kibera-residents-reach-Canaan-5816.html" rel="nofollow">(Capital FM)</a></li>
<li>21 people are injured, three seriously, after a collision involving a <a href="/wiki/Luas" title="Luas">Luas</a> tram and a double-decker bus on <a href="/wiki/O%27Connell_Street" title="O'Connell Street">O'Connell Street</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>, the worst ever accident involving the city's trams. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0916/breaking50.html?via=mr" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0916/luas.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.belfasttelegraph.co.uk/breaking-news/ireland/at-least-16-injured-in-dublin-busluas-crash-14495297.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Belfast Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5hFu6mhrpWVkj9fuHtzD4YqpHUDGw" rel="nofollow">(The Canadian Press)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/TEAMS_(cable_system)" title="TEAMS (cable system)">TEAMS cable system</a>, providing high speed <a href="/wiki/Broadband" title="Broadband">broadband</a> to <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">East Africa</a> for the first time, is poised to go live. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/technology/8257038.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> border guards shoot dead two sub-<a href="/wiki/Sahara" title="Sahara">Saharan</a> migrants, bringing to at least 14 the number killed this year as they try to cross illegally into <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=85&amp;art_id=nw20090916100524369C781493" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A lightning bolt kills five children at their school in <a href="/wiki/Bamali" title="Bamali">Bamali</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a>, as they are preparing to begin their school day. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090916224016183C394875" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_17&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A senior <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Irish</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Catholic" title="Catholic">Catholic</a> <a href="/wiki/Bishop" title="Bishop">bishop</a> says <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholics</a> can vote "Yes" in the country's <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">second referendum</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> "in good conscience". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8260836.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>At least 87 refugees are killed after an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yemen_Army" title="Yemen Army">army</a> air raid on a camp for displaced people in <a href="/wiki/%27Amran_Governorate" title="'Amran Governorate">'Amran Governorate</a>, northern <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/8260414.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sabanews.net/en/news193895.htm" rel="nofollow">(Saba)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bernama.com/bernama/v5/newsworld.php?id=441164" rel="nofollow">(Bernama)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/2009917172952710277.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> says <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> leaders agree to impose a cap on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Banking" title="Banking">banker</a> pay. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gp8M6dmt8Ho2DRK_eqR7dl7QsMXAD9AP9HRG3" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="Prime Minister of the Czech Republic">Prime Minister of the Czech Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jan_Fischer_(politician)" title="Jan Fischer (politician)">Jan Fischer</a>, says that <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> told him that the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> is abandoning plans for a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Missile_shield" title="Missile shield">missile shield</a> based in <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/6623084.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20090917/156157221.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>Two large explosions hit the main base of <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> peacekeepers in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/world/59606497.html?elr=KArks:DCiUBcy7hUiacyKUUr" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Chicago Star-Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/17/content_12070226.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shia_insurgency_in_Yemen" title="Shia insurgency in Yemen">Shia insurgency in Yemen</a>: More than 80 people are killed in an air raid on a camp for displaced people in northern <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/8260414.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A number of children are injured in <a href="/wiki/Ansbach_school_attack" title="Ansbach school attack">an attack at the Carolinum secondary school</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">Bavarian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Ansbach" title="Ansbach">Ansbach</a>. <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> police arrest a man. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8260427.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0917/germany.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a> says it would consider quitting <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Union of South American Nations">UNASUR</a> if the bloc does not agree to debate issues related to <a href="/wiki/Illegal_drug_trade" title="Illegal drug trade">drug trafficking</a>, <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a> and arms purchases. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/17/isolated-colombia-seriously-considering-abandoning-unasur" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_government_of_Ethiopia" title="List of heads of government of Ethiopia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Meles_Zenawi" title="Meles Zenawi">Meles Zenawi</a> denounces an <a href="/wiki/International_Crisis_Group" title="International Crisis Group">International Crisis Group</a> (ICG) report that warns his country could descend into ethnic violence ahead of its first national election since a 2005 poll triggered deadly street clashes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090917101252698C892021" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A large <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> attack in the centre of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, kills six <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISAF" title="ISAF">ISAF</a> soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8260419.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.adnkronos.com/AKI/English/Security/?id=3.0.3780942288" rel="nofollow">(Adnkronos)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>'s top <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamic</a> authority, <a href="/wiki/Grand_Mufti" title="Grand Mufti">Grand Mufti</a> <a href="/wiki/Ali_Gomaa" title="Ali Gomaa">Ali Gomaa</a>, defends women's rights to wear trousers in public following the high-profile court case in neighbouring <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> where women, including <a href="/wiki/Lubna_al-Hussein" title="Lubna al-Hussein">Lubna al-Hussein</a>, were <a href="/wiki/Flagellation" title="Flagellation">flogged</a> for dressing in the garments. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=85&amp;art_id=nw20090916223934870C716625" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Seven explosions hit the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burmese</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Yangon" title="Yangon">Yangon</a> with no casualties. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/asia/154688/seven-bomb-blasts-in-burma-no-casualties-police" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/rest-of-world/Series-of-explosions-hit-Myanmars-biggest-city/articleshow/5022187.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> police confirm the death of their most wanted man, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Noordin_Mohammed_Top" title="Noordin Mohammed Top">Noordin Mohammed Top</a>, who was suspected of involvement in the <a href="/wiki/2009_Jakarta_bombings" title="2009 Jakarta bombings">2009 Jakarta bombings</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2002_Bali_bombings" title="2002 Bali bombings">Bali bombings</a> in 2002. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2009/09/17/police-confirm-noordin%E2%80%99s-death.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/200991783135850613.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/asiapcf/09/17/indonesia.terror.raid/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> Under-Secretary General for <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Department_of_Political_Affairs" title="United Nations Department of Political Affairs">Political Affairs</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lynn_Pascoe" title="Lynn Pascoe">Lynn Pascoe</a> begins visiting camps holding displaced <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tamil_people" title="Tamil people">Tamil</a> refugees in northern <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.colombopage.com/archive_091/Sep1253162909CH.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Colombo Page</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/8260294.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jsdaU0jbLr79D4V9KgAam7E3nf2A" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> agree a <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">$</a>16 billion oil exploration deal allowing China to drill in the <a href="/wiki/Orinoco" title="Orinoco">Orinoco</a> basin. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601086&amp;sid=aR9vgkncL_A4" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/venezuela-china-agree-16-billion-oil-deal-2009-09-17" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2009/09/200991741755683835.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The ruling Burmese <a href="/wiki/State_Peace_and_Development_Council" title="State Peace and Development Council">junta</a> defends its decision to bar opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a> from attending her appeal hearing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/SE%2BAsia/Story/STIStory_431022.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.gulfnews.com/world/Myanmar/10349727.html" rel="nofollow">(Gulf News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/Article.aspx?articleId=506072&amp;publicationSubCategoryId=200" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Star</i>)</a></li>
<li>Four more people are found guilty and jailed for carrying out <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/September_2009_Xinjiang_attacks" title="September 2009 Xinjiang attacks">attacks with syringes</a> in the western <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> province of <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8261169.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Kenya" title="National Assembly of Kenya">National Assembly of Kenya</a> passes a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bill_(proposed_law)" title="Bill (proposed law)">bill</a> to reduce the number of ministries from 40 to 24. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8260811.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_18&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_18&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
