<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Two people are killed and eight are hurt when a man confronted by police for scrawling graffiti at a <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a> <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City_Metro" title="Mexico City Metro">Metro station</a> opens fire on passers-by. <a class="external text" href="http://us.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/americas/09/19/mexico.subway.shooting/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8264340.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/gunman-opens-fire-in-mexico-subway-20090919-fvy5.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Wujek-Slask_mine_blast" title="2009 Wujek-Slask mine blast">mine blast</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ruda_%C5%9Al%C4%85ska" title="Ruda Śląska">Ruda Śląska</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, kills at least 13 miners and hospitalises at least 30 more. The country's worst mining disaster since 2006, two days of national mourning are declared the following day. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/8264624.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2009/09/2009918145056895158.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0918/breaking51.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> sentences former <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Stanley" title="Morgan Stanley">Morgan Stanley</a> managing director <a href="/wiki/Du_Jun" title="Du Jun">Du Jun</a> to seven years in prison for his <a href="/wiki/Insider_trading" title="Insider trading">insider trading</a> conviction in its most high-profile case. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8262627.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Quds_Day" title="International Quds Day">International Quds Day</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iran" title="President of Iran">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">Mahmoud Ahmadinejad</a> calls <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a> a "<a href="/wiki/Holocaust_denial" title="Holocaust denial">myth</a>" and says that "the very existence of this regime is an insult to the dignity of the people" in referring to <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> at a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Quds_Day" title="International Quds Day">Quds Day</a> rally in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0918/iran.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/18/content_12075949.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/18/opposition-protests-iran-quds-day" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Pro and anti-government protestors clash in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> during the annual <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Quds_Day" title="International Quds Day">International Quds Day</a> rally. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/200991875246806121.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/8262273.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/18/content_12076522.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=106528&amp;sectionid=351020101" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_German_foreign_ministers" title="List of German foreign ministers">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Frank-Walter_Steinmeier" title="Frank-Walter Steinmeier">Frank-Walter Steinmeier</a> condemns Ahmadinejad's remarks, calling him a disgrace to his country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE58H4WE20090918" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>30,000 <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a> residents seriously affected by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2006_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire_toxic_waste_dump" title="2006 Côte d'Ivoire toxic waste dump">dumping of toxic waste by Trafigura</a>, which, according to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, has killed at least 15 people, say an undisclosed compensation deal offered by a <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>-based oil firm is not enough. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8261668.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Solidarity_(Polish_trade_union)" title="Solidarity (Polish trade union)">Solidarity</a> co-founder and former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Poland" title="President of Poland">President of Poland</a> <a href="/wiki/Lech_Wa%C5%82%C4%99sa" title="Lech Wałęsa">Lech Wałęsa</a> (in favour) and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Independence_Party" title="United Kingdom Independence Party">United Kingdom Independence Party</a> (UKIP) leader <a href="/wiki/Nigel_Farage" title="Nigel Farage">Nigel Farage</a> (against) arrive in <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> to campaign over the country's <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">second referendum</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2009/09/18/walesa-backs-ireland-s-lisbon-referendum-yes/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/ireland/2009/0919/1224254861207.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/ireland/article6840682.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a> begins releasing 7,114 prisoners in an <a href="/wiki/Amnesty" title="Amnesty">amnesty</a> announced by the government. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/200991804654921820.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hUWldouqQgO9AgCD-WKY-o5Tt-xA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li>A Burmese court announces it is to reveal its verdict on an appeal by <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a> in October. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/SE%2BAsia/Story/STIStory_431509.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5iCrk3lf8VHAA4vSqllC6wi6UVNzgD9APLNMO2" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8262175.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The first ever <a href="/wiki/Global_Irish_Economic_Forum" title="Global Irish Economic Forum">Global Irish Economic Forum</a>, modelled on <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>'s <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a>, begins in <a href="/wiki/Farmleigh" title="Farmleigh">Farmleigh</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_Park" title="Phoenix Park">Phoenix Park</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.belfasttelegraph.co.uk/breaking-news/ireland/irish-global-economic-forum-in-dublin-today-14499744.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Belfast Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/finance/2009/0918/1224254786972.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0918/forum-business.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.forbes.com/feeds/reuters/2009/09/18/2009-09-18T182942Z_01_LI359383_RTRIDST_0_IRELAND-FORUM-UPDATE-1.html" rel="nofollow">(Forbes)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/marketsNews/idUSLI35938320090918" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Brazil" title="Government of Brazil">government</a> announces a plan to ban <a href="/wiki/Sugarcane" title="Sugarcane">sugarcane</a> farming in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amazon_Rainforest" title="Amazon Rainforest">Amazon Rainforest</a> and indigenous areas. <a class="external text" href="http://www.laht.com/article.asp?ArticleId=343940&amp;CategoryId=14090" rel="nofollow">(<i>Latin American Herald Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8262381.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a> tells a visiting envoy of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="President of the People's Republic of China">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hu_Jintao" title="Hu Jintao">Hu Jintao</a> he is willing to engage in talks on his country's nuclear programme. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8262223.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/northkorea/2009/09/18/89/0401000000AEN20090918005300315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguayan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Uruguay" title="List of Presidents of Uruguay">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Tabar%C3%A9_V%C3%A1zquez" title="Tabaré Vázquez">Tabaré Vázquez</a> calls for an integrated <a href="/wiki/Mercosur" title="Mercosur">Mercosur</a> with a greater number of countries to make it more competitive overseas, but also demands greater balance inside the group among members. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/18/uruguayan-president-calls-for-stronger-and-more-balanced-mercosur" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> announces it will rehouse displaced <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tamil_people" title="Tamil people">Tamil</a> refugees within the next four months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gVNiGMpt-BWgkDw-mzMBxz9bAHzAD9APN7D81" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Office" title="Foreign and Commonwealth Office">Foreign and Commonwealth Office</a> confirms that serving <a href="/wiki/Police_Service_of_Northern_Ireland" title="Police Service of Northern Ireland">PSNI</a> officers provided training to the <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> police force in the past twelve months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0918/libya.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Two people are killed and a further 12 injured in a stabbing attack in <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2009-09/18/content_8709175.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hvHDpk9Y7f1LmT0RfNYMg3CxKzCAD9APIP9G0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinapost.com.tw/china/local-news/beijing/2009/09/18/225242/Man-stabs.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 33 people die as a result of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomb" title="Suicide bomb">suicide bomb</a> attack in <a href="/wiki/Kohat" title="Kohat">Kohat</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa" title="Khyber Pakhtunkhwa">North West Frontier Province</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0918/pakistan.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hkiMxbHNH0BqgpWA2ZG6VD6wVTmAD9APJ60G2" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8262199.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=126&amp;art_id=nw20090919174408965C367874" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nicola_Roxon" title="Nicola Roxon">Nicola Roxon</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Health_and_Aged_Care" title="Minister for Health and Aged Care">Minister for Health and Ageing</a>, says that the <a href="/wiki/Therapeutic_Goods_Administration" title="Therapeutic Goods Administration">Therapeutic Goods Administration</a> has approved an Australian-made <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Swine_flu" title="Swine flu">swine flu</a> <a href="/wiki/Vaccine" title="Vaccine">vaccine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.fox59.com/news/nationworld/sns-ap-as-australia-swine-flu,0,7827983.story" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox 59)</a></li>
<li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Raptorex" title="Raptorex">Raptorex kriegsteini</a></i>, a smaller version of the <i><a href="/wiki/Tyrannosaurus" title="Tyrannosaurus">Tyrannosaurus rex</a></i>, is discovered in northeastern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/science/dinosaurs/6201316/Tinysaurus-Rex-just-nine-foot-long-and-weighing-the-same-as-a-human-discovered.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/17/AR2009091702573.html?hpid=sec-nation" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/science/2009/sep/17/tiny-t-rex-fossil" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> says a <a href="/wiki/2009_African_Union_base_bombings_in_Mogadishu" title="2009 African Union base bombings in Mogadishu">twin bombing</a> that killed 17 peacekeepers on its base in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>, was conducted in <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">UN</a> marked cars. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/africa/09/18/somalia.suicide.attack/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090918121524565C823719" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Michel_Bagaragaza&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Michel Bagaragaza (page does not exist)">Michel Bagaragaza</a>, former head of <a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwanda</a>'s tea industry, pleads guilty to complicity in the 1994 genocide, altering his original not guilty plea. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8262368.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>'s best-known watercolour artist, <a href="/wiki/Cultural_Medallion" title="Cultural Medallion">Cultural Medallion</a> recipient <a href="/wiki/Ong_Kim_Seng" title="Ong Kim Seng">Ong Kim Seng</a>, donates eight works to the country's new national art gallery. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Singapore/Story/STIStory_431682.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_19&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A six-nation east <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">African</a> regional bloc consisting of <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">Djibouti</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a> urges global sanctions on <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a> for backing <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamist</a> rebels in neighbouring war-torn Somalia. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090919203432132C615052" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Two men are arrested in <a href="/wiki/Denver" title="Denver">Denver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, as part of an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FBI" title="FBI">FBI</a> terror probe. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gT-Kwm3eHQPp5qw5B5yzpuy07XuwD9AQRJPG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Attacks by rebels in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> are reported despite a <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/meast/09/19/yemen.cease.fire/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sabanews.net/en/news193980.htm" rel="nofollow">(Saba)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8265134.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/People%27s_Alliance_for_Democracy" title="People's Alliance for Democracy">Pro</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_United_Front_of_Democracy_Against_Dictatorship" title="National United Front of Democracy Against Dictatorship">anti</a> government protestors demonstrate in the <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a> and near the <a href="/wiki/Preah_Vihear_Temple" title="Preah Vihear Temple">Preah Vihear Temple</a> along the border with <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/local/24102/suthep-warns-over-rally" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8264189.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/19/content_12080244.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Gay_pride" title="Gay pride">gay pride</a> march in <a href="/wiki/Belgrade" title="Belgrade">Belgrade</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>, is called off after police and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Serbia" title="List of Prime Ministers of Serbia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Mirko_Cvetkovi%C4%87" title="Mirko Cvetković">Mirko Cvetković</a> tell organisers they could not guarantee its safety. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8264514.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/europe/Serbias-gay-parade-cancelled-after-threats/articleshow/5031052.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory?id=8619023" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> measuring 5.8 on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Richter_scale" title="Richter scale">Richter scale</a> occurs off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Bali" title="Bali">Bali</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8264169.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/DNA" title="DNA">DNA</a> tests confirm that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> <a href="/wiki/Bomb" title="Bomb">bomber</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Noordin_Mohamed_Top" title="Noordin Mohamed Top">Noordin Mohamed Top</a> is dead. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8264190.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_European_Commission" title="President of the European Commission">President of the European Commission</a> <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Manuel_Barroso" title="José Manuel Barroso">José Manuel Barroso</a> arrives in <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> on the campaign trail for the country's <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">second referendum</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0919/eulisbon.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE58I0KE20090919" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/ireland/article6840613.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> warns the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a> it will have to face the “consequences” if <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="President of the Czech Republic">President</a> <a href="/wiki/V%C3%A1clav_Klaus" title="Václav Klaus">Václav Klaus</a> refuses to sign the Lisbon Treaty allowing it to enter into force. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/world/2009/0919/1224254860514.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Four people are seriously injured in a bear attack in <a href="/wiki/Takayama,_Gifu" title="Takayama, Gifu">Takayama</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gifu_Prefecture" title="Gifu Prefecture">Gifu Prefecture</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8265084.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> police raid a local <a href="/wiki/Security" title="Security">security</a> firm that provides security for the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> embassy for illegal weapons possession. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/6626569.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> government raises its terrorism alert level after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda" title="Al Qaeda">al Qaeda</a> posted a video on the Internet threatening attacks in <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> based on the outcome of this month's elections. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/europe/09/18/germany.alqaeda/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> ships become the first Western commercial vessels to navigate the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Sea_Route" title="Northern Sea Route">Northern Sea Route</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8264345.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Singer <a href="/wiki/Vera_Lynn" title="Vera Lynn">Vera Lynn</a>, aged 92, becomes the oldest artist to obtain a number one <a href="/wiki/Album" title="Album">album</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/19/world/europe/19iht-letter.html?ref=world" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>'s government holds emergency talks with farmers to avert protests over falling dairy prices. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8265109.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope" title="Pope">Pope</a> <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI" title="Pope Benedict XVI">Benedict XVI</a> announces he is to hold a special meeting of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a> <a href="/wiki/Bishop" title="Bishop">bishops</a> to discuss the concerns and challenges of the Church in the <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle East</a> in October 2010. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0919/breaking38.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>'s government asks cinemas to stop showing the science fiction film, <i><a href="/wiki/District_9" title="District 9">District 9</a></i>, saying it denigrates the country's image by portraying Nigerians as cannibals, criminals and prostitutes. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8264180.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Hundreds of <a href="/wiki/Parachuting" title="Parachuting">parachutists</a> from the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> commemorate the 65th anniversary of <a href="/wiki/Operation_Market_Garden" title="Operation Market Garden">Operation Market Garden</a> near <a href="/wiki/Arnhem" title="Arnhem">Arnhem</a>, the Netherlands. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/the-battle-of-arnhem-remembered-20090919-fw7n.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Becky Simmons becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Guernsey" title="Guernsey">Guernsey</a>-born person to swim the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thisisguernsey.com/2009/09/21/channel-conquered/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guernsey Press</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Trafigura" title="Trafigura">Trafigura</a> oil trading firm agrees to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2006_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire_toxic_waste_dump" title="2006 Côte d'Ivoire toxic waste dump">pay more than $46 million compensation</a> to more than 30,000 people in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire" title="Côte d'Ivoire">Côte d'Ivoire</a> who say they were made ill by dumped waste in 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8265193.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/2009920132129567154.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/trafigura-settles-over-ivory-coast-toxic-waste-claims-20090920-fwut.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSLK593911" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20090920-ivory-coast-toxic-waste-dumping-trafigura-reaches-settlement-claims" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/africa/article6839258.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>More than 140 <a href="/wiki/Shia_Islam" title="Shia Islam">Shiite</a> Houthi rebels are killed in northern <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> after they attempt to take over the government palace in the city of <a href="/wiki/Sa%27dah" title="Sa'dah">Sa'dah</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sabanews.net/en/news194060.htm" rel="nofollow">(Yemen News Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iydUqVjH6TUmobVgoVJqsIgg8iuA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=106684&amp;sectionid=351020206" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Plaza_de_la_Revoluci%C3%B3n" title="Plaza de la Revolución">Plaza de la Revolución</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juanes" title="Juanes">Juanes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Silvio Rodríguez">Silvio Rodríguez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miguel_Bos%C3%A9" title="Miguel Bosé">Miguel Bosé</a> headline <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>'s largest open-air concert since the <a href="/wiki/Cuban_Revolution" title="Cuban Revolution">1959 Revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.granma.cu/ingles/2009/septiembre/domingo20/palabras-i.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Granma</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8265177.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jjPq22GvQrQscxHfi5FGRTLOAlMgD9AR6CH00" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Colombia" title="President of Colombia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Uribe" title="Álvaro Uribe">Álvaro Uribe</a> eases the terms for the release of 24 police and soldiers being held by <a href="/wiki/Marxism" title="Marxism">Marxist</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Armed_Forces_of_Colombia" title="Revolutionary Armed Forces of Colombia">FARC</a> rebels. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8265167.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of Congo">Democratic Republic of Congo</a> transfers <a href="/wiki/Gr%C3%A9goire_Ndahimana" title="Grégoire Ndahimana">Grégoire Ndahimana</a> to the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_Rwanda" title="International Criminal Tribunal for Rwanda">International Criminal Tribunal for Rwanda</a> (ICTR) to stand trial for the massacre of at least 2,000 <a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwandan</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tutsis" title="Tutsis">Tutsis</a> during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rwandan_Genocide" title="Rwandan Genocide">1994 genocide</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/idUKTRE58J1E520090920" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Ireland" title="Government of Ireland">Government of Ireland</a> approves the introduction of a national <a href="/wiki/Postal_code" title="Postal code">postal code</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0920/postcode.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Tribesmen attack a village in south <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, overwhelming soldiers guarding the settlement and killing an unknown number. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=136&amp;art_id=nw20090920230334122C574551" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(Somalia)" title="Al-Shabaab (Somalia)">al-Shabaab</a> insurgents warn schools not to use textbooks provided by <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> agencies and other donors they accuse of being un-<a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamic</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090920110936634C756282" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8265559.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/somalia/6211720/Somali-insurgents-warn-schools-not-to-use-UN-textbooks.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/20/AR2009092000312.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The bust of a <a href="/wiki/Sumer" title="Sumer">Sumerian</a> king is among eight stolen antiques recovered in an undercover operation by <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> police. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8265265.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 21, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-21</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_21&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_21&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A trial against former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> <a href="/wiki/Dominique_de_Villepin" title="Dominique de Villepin">Dominique de Villepin</a>, over the <a href="/wiki/Clearstream#The_Clearstream_affair" title="Clearstream">Clearstream affair</a>, begins in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8266001.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0921/devillepin.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/france/6211765/Clearstream-Frances-trial-of-the-century-begins.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/20/sarkozy-de-villepin-clearstream-trial" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Macanese_legislative_election,_2009" title="Macanese legislative election, 2009">Legislative elections</a> in <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a> attract a higher turnout than usual and strengthen the democratic minority. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8266060.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.radioaustralianews.net.au/stories/200909/2691926.htm?desktop" rel="nofollow">(Radio Australia News)</a></li>
<li>Ousted <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduran</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a> returns to his country, almost three months after the coup which overthrew him. He seeks shelter in the <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Brazil" title="List of diplomatic missions of Brazil">Brazilian embassy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Tegucigalpa" title="Tegucigalpa">Tegucigalpa</a>. Interim president <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Micheletti" title="Roberto Micheletti">Roberto Micheletti</a> orders a 26 hour <a href="/wiki/Curfew" title="Curfew">curfew</a> and shuts down the airport as a result of the demonstrations sparked by Zelaya's return. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8267775.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/21/ousted-zelaya-in-back-in-honduras-and-calls-for-dialogue" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hb3LUciR3gBHn6x7f4BBQHIPYZPQD9ARV9683" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hb3LUciR3gBHn6x7f4BBQHIPYZPQD9AS3F901" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE58K3JY20090921" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/2009_Bhutan_earthquake" title="2009 Bhutan earthquake">6.1 magnitude earthquake</a> occurs in eastern <a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a> and is felt in northeast <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region" title="Tibet Autonomous Region">Tibet</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>, leaving at least 10 dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.earthtimes.org/articles/show/286603,seven-dead-as-quake-rocks-bhutan-india-and-tibet--summary.html" rel="nofollow">(Earth Times)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/asiapcf/09/21/bhutan.quake/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.indianexpress.com/news/earthquake-kills-at-least-7-in-bhutan-shakes-assam/519737/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Indian Express</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbs.com.bt/Earthquake%20hits%20Bhutan.html" rel="nofollow">(BBS)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2009/9/21/apworld/20090921173152&amp;sec=apworld" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Star</i>)</a></li>
<li>A passenger train is intentionally derailed near <a href="/wiki/Craiova" title="Craiova">Craiova</a>, <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, injuring many people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.roumanie.com/romania-news-1001739.html" rel="nofollow">(Roumanie.com)</a></li>
<li>New clashes break out in the <a href="/wiki/Darfur" title="Darfur">Darfur</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8266314.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.etaiwannews.com/etn/news_content.php?id=1062219&amp;lang=eng_news" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taiwan News</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South African</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Africa" title="President of South Africa">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Zuma" title="Jacob Zuma">Jacob Zuma</a> admits disagreements do exist between the <a href="/wiki/African_National_Congress" title="African National Congress">ANC</a> and the trade union federation (<a href="/wiki/Congress_of_South_African_Trade_Unions" title="Congress of South African Trade Unions">COSATU</a>)—one of its main political partners. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8267168.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> holds a <a href="/wiki/State_funeral" title="State funeral">state funeral</a> for six soldiers killed in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> last week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5gSM5ghQShu5GtxfCo7fFMO8M_BlAD9ARKD5G0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.adnkronos.com/AKI/English/Security/?id=3.0.3794455127" rel="nofollow">(Adnkronos)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s first <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Boris_Yeltsin" title="Boris Yeltsin">Boris Yeltsin</a> spent his retirement in a "golden cage", his phone tapped and the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Russia" title="Government of Russia">Kremlin</a> controlling visitors, a colleague reveals. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0921/breaking47.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Sir Alex Ferguson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gary_Lineker" title="Gary Lineker">Gary Lineker</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a> are among 1,000 guests at a memorial service held for the recently deceased <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football manager</a> <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Robson" title="Bobby Robson">Sir Bobby Robson</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/sport/football/international/article6842948.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/football-stars-pay-final-tribute-to-sir-bobby-20090922-fyqr.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/sports/soccer/2009-09-21-1408159171_x.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>Most of the world's major <a href="/wiki/River_delta" title="River delta">river deltas</a> are sinking, including <a href="/wiki/Colorado_River" title="Colorado River">Colorado</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nile" title="Nile">Nile</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pearl_River_(China)" title="Pearl River (China)">Pearl</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rhone" title="Rhone">Rhone</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yangtze_River" title="Yangtze River">Yangtze</a>, increasing the flood risk faced by ½ a billion people, scientists report. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/science/nature/8266500.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>New figures released by the Japanese <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Japan" title="Government of Japan">government</a> indicate one in four women are aged 65 or over for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantoday.com/category/national/view/1-in-4-women-in-japan-now-aged-65-or-older-govt-estimate" rel="nofollow">(Japan Today)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://mdn.mainichi.jp/mdnnews/news/20090921p2a00m0na014000c.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Mainichi Shimbun</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jVBVBm_bBDfvqMS9IFZtXwCcOmvQ" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nuer_people" title="Nuer people">Lou Nuer</a> militiamen kill more than 100 civilians and security force members in an attack in <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>'s <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Duk_Padiet&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Duk Padiet (page does not exist)">Duk Padiet</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jonglei" title="Jonglei">Jonglei</a>, the latest in a series of ethnic clashes. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8267308.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A judicial official says a 51-year-old man has confessed to sending threatening letters containing bullets to <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> and other prominent figures. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=3&amp;art_id=nw20090921141509152C345961" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>In <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Long_distance_swimming" title="Long distance swimming">swimming</a>, Lisa Cummins becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Irish</a> person and the 20th person ever to complete a two way crossing of the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/swimming/2009/0921/cumminsl.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ Sport)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0921/breaking65.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.kentonline.co.uk/kentonline/news/2009/september/21/irish_womans_corking_effort.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Kent Online)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puma_AG" title="Puma AG">Puma</a> end their 60-year-old feud. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/8267709.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Singer <a href="/wiki/Jade_Ewen" title="Jade Ewen">Jade Ewen</a> is confirmed as the new member of <a href="/wiki/Sugababes_discography" title="Sugababes discography">internationally successful</a> girlband <a href="/wiki/Sugababes" title="Sugababes">Sugababes</a>, replacing the only original member <a href="/wiki/Keisha_Buchanan" title="Keisha Buchanan">Keisha Buchanan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1215134/Keisha-quits-Sugababes-NOT-Amelle-says-It-choice-leave.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Massimo_Busacca" title="Massimo Busacca">Massimo Busacca</a>, a high-profile <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Swiss</a> football referee who officiated the <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2009 UEFA Champions League Final">2009 UEFA Champions League Final</a> and was expected to take part at the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>, is suspended "immediately" for waving his middle finger at fans during a match. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8268036.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Rescuers scour the sea off the <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> coast for dozens of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">African</a> migrants who are missing and feared dead after their boat capsized in an accident that kills eight others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090920225823356C781200" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2009/09/20/2691011.htm?section=world" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/20/content_12083963.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>American <a href="/wiki/Mesac_Damas" title="Mesac Damas">Mesac Damas</a> is extradited from <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a> to stand trial for the murders of his six family members in <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USA" title="USA">USA</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.nbc-2.com/global/story.asp?s=11181238" rel="nofollow">NBC-2</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Iranian_Air_Force_mid-air_collision" title="2009 Iranian Air Force mid-air collision">mid-air collision</a> destroys <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>'s only <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Airborne_Early_Warning_and_Control" title="Airborne Early Warning and Control">AWACS</a> equipped aircraft, an <a href="/wiki/Ilyushin_Il-76" title="Ilyushin Il-76">Ilyushin Il-76</a>MD. (<a class="external text" href="http://www2.debka.com/headline.php?hid=6280" rel="nofollow">Debka</a>), (<a class="external text" href="http://www.defensenews.com/story.php?i=4289949&amp;c=AIR&amp;s=MID" rel="nofollow">Defensenews</a>)</li>
<li>A gang of <a href="/wiki/Racism" title="Racism">racist</a> youths are sent to jail for a string of attacks on foreigners in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, in 2008. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8269645.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduran</a> soldiers break up protests outside the <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> embassy in <a href="/wiki/Tegucigalpa" title="Tegucigalpa">Tegucigalpa</a> in support of deposed <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a>, who is staying inside. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8269073.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/22/honduran-de-facto-rulers-demand-brazil-hand-over-zelaya" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>

<li>New figures reveal that for the first time since 1995 more people emigrated from <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> than immigrated there, with a growth of more than 40% from January–April 2009. Most of the emigrants are <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Europe" title="Eastern Europe">Eastern European</a> or Irish nationals. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0922/cso1.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>

<li>The U.S. <a href="/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="Food and Drug Administration">Food and Drug Administration</a> bans the sale of flavored cigarettes, except for <a href="/wiki/Menthol_cigarette" title="Menthol cigarette">menthol cigarettes</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/23/health/policy/23fda.html?_r=1&amp;hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York TImes</i>)</a></li>

<ul>
<li>The cities of <a href="/wiki/Canberra" title="Canberra">Canberra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brisbane" title="Brisbane">Brisbane</a> in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> are covered by a <a href="/wiki/2009_Australian_dust_storm" title="2009 Australian dust storm">dust storm</a>, the worst in at least 70 years. Aviation in <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a> is disrupted. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,26113952-5006784,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2009/09/23/2694051.htm?section=australia" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.canberratimes.com.au/news/local/news/general/dust-hail-and-deluge/1630629.aspx" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Canberra Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/2009_Korba_chimney_collapse" title="2009 Korba chimney collapse">chimney collapse</a> in <a href="/wiki/Korba,_Chhattisgarh" title="Korba, Chhattisgarh">Korba</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_India" title="States and territories of India">Indian state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Chhattisgarh" title="Chhattisgarh">Chhattisgarh</a> leaves at least 15 workers dead and at least 50 feared trapped. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8271423.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> government pitches a tent in suburban <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a> on land rented from <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> that leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> may use for entertaining, but local officials order workers to stop the construction, saying it "violated several codes and laws of the town of <a href="/wiki/Bedford_(town),_New_York" title="Bedford (town), New York">Bedford</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/gadhafis-trump-card-a-tent-in-new-york-20090923-g1oz.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/us_and_americas/article6845459.ece#cid=OTC-RSS&amp;attr=797093" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8270450.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.scmp.com/vgn-ext-templating/v/index.jsp?vgnextoid=ae43ca15365e3210VgnVCM100000360a0a0aRCRD&amp;s=News&amp;ss=Asia+%26+World" rel="nofollow">(<i>South China Morning Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/world/news/article.cfm?c_id=2&amp;objectid=10599135&amp;ref=rss" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Bhutan" title="List of Prime Ministers of Bhutan">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a> <a href="/wiki/Jigme_Thinley" title="Jigme Thinley">Jigme Thinley</a> describes an earthquake which hit the Himalayan kingdom on Monday as "one of the biggest disasters in recent times". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8270418.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Gay activists in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a> welcome a life sentence for a man involved in the gang rape and murder of <a href="/wiki/Lesbian" title="Lesbian">lesbian</a> <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> star <a href="/wiki/Eudy_Simelane" title="Eudy Simelane">Eudy Simelane</a>, one of the first women to openly live as a lesbian in her community of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/KwaThema,_Gauteng" title="KwaThema, Gauteng">KwaThema</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8270417.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Cuba" title="President of Cuba">President of Cuba</a> <a href="/wiki/Fidel_Castro" title="Fidel Castro">Fidel Castro</a> praises current <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> for his speech before the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> for admitting it had been slow to act on climate change but urges that the American capitalist system is incompatible with a clean planet. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8272013.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>One of the busiest border crossings between <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Ysidro,_San_Diego,_California" title="San Ysidro, San Diego, California">San Ysidro</a> is closed for hours after a gun battle between US agents and suspected human traffickers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8270147.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/22/AR2009092204511.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post'</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/world/us-closes-border-crossing-with-mexico-after-shootout/story-e6frf7lf-1225778726559?from=public_rss" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scottish</a> £1 banknote, dated 1836, sells for a world record £9,000 price at auction. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/scotland/8270511.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Swedish</a> police hunt for robbers who used a stolen helicopter to raid a cash depot in <a href="/wiki/Stockholm" title="Stockholm">Stockholm</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0923/sweden.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8270619.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A report carried by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sydney_Morning_Herald" title="The Sydney Morning Herald">The Sydney Morning Herald</a></i> says <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> is poised to be the world's fastest growing industrialised nation over the next four decades, reaching a population of 35 million by 2050. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/world/news/article.cfm?c_id=2&amp;objectid=10599073" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Police_(Germany)" title="Federal Police (Germany)">Bundespolizei</a> investigate whether a string of letters from the <a href="/wiki/National_Democratic_Party_of_Germany" title="National Democratic Party of Germany">far-right NPD party</a> to politicians from <a href="/wiki/Immigration" title="Immigration">immigrant</a> backgrounds have incited <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_hatred" title="Ethnic hatred">racial hatred</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8270598.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,4713188,00.html?maca=en-currentaffairs_germany-77-rdf" rel="nofollow">(Deusche Welle)</a></li>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a> sentences three men to death by hanging for killing a 14-year-old <a href="/wiki/Albinism" title="Albinism">albino</a> boy, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Matatizo_Dunia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Matatizo Dunia (page does not exist)">Matatizo Dunia</a>, to steal parts of his anatomy. It is the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Persecution_of_albinism" title="Persecution of albinism">country's first conviction</a> for this offence. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8270446.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A man is shot dead in a clash between police and supporters of ousted <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduran</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a>, believed to be the first death since his return to the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0923/honduras.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> villagers accuse the actress <a href="/wiki/Julia_Roberts" title="Julia Roberts">Julia Roberts</a> of interrupting <a href="/wiki/Navratri" title="Navratri">Navratri</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8270556.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> successfully launches seven satellites in a single mission one month after its inaugural <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">Moon</a> mission is aborted. Included are six smaller satellites from <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/8270200.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?from=rss_Space&amp;set_id=1&amp;click_id=118&amp;art_id=nw20090923114247185C548138" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Julio_Alberto_Poch&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Julio Alberto Poch (page does not exist)">Julio Alberto Poch</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Transavia" title="Transavia">Transavia</a> commercial airline pilot, is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> over his alleged role in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>'s 1976–1983 "<a href="/wiki/Dirty_War" title="Dirty War">Dirty War</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8271341.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/23/death-flights-pilot-arrest-argentina" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/us_and_americas/article6845817.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/news/world/AP/story/1247252.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Miami Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/idUKTRE58M1KF20090923?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>In his first <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> appearance, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> calls for reform of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Security_Council" title="Security Council">Security Council</a> and chastises the Council for failing to intervene or prevent some 65 wars since the U.N. was founded in 1945. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/32986087/ns/world_news-united_nations/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> relaxes travel curbs for <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a> residents visiting <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_433476.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> urges world leaders to call on <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> to free hundreds of thousands of displaced people detained in camps since the island's civil war ended. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/Breaking%2BNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_433373.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Polish</a> court awards €7,400 damages to <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Alicja_Tysi%C4%85c&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Alicja Tysiąc (page does not exist)">Alicja Tysiąc</a>, likened to a child killer and <a href="/wiki/Nazism" title="Nazism">Nazi</a> war criminal by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Catholic" title="Catholic">Catholic</a> magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Go%C5%9B%C4%87_Niedzielny" title="Gość Niedzielny">Gość Niedzielny</a></i> for wanting an <a href="/wiki/Abortion" title="Abortion">abortion</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8271895.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>'s first <a href="/wiki/Naturism" title="Naturism">nudist</a> hiking trail opens. <a class="external text" href="http://www.spiegel.de/international/zeitgeist/0,1518,650329,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Der Spiegel</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/travel/travel-news/nude-hikers-get-their-own-trail-in-germany-20090923-g27l.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/oddlyEnoughNews/idINTRE58L3PR20090922?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=oddlyEnoughNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/32966748/ns/world_news-europe/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ABBA" title="ABBA">ABBA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Genesis_(band)" title="Genesis (band)">Genesis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kiss_(band)" title="Kiss (band)">Kiss</a>, <a href="/wiki/LL_Cool_J" title="LL Cool J">LL Cool J</a>, <a href="/wiki/Red_Hot_Chili_Peppers" title="Red Hot Chili Peppers">Red Hot Chili Peppers</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Stooges" title="The Stooges">The Stooges</a> are amongst several acts nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame" title="Rock and Roll Hall of Fame">Rock and Roll Hall of Fame</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rollingstone.com/rockdaily/index.php/2009/09/23/red-hot-chili-peppers-ll-cool-j-kiss-lead-2010-rock-and-roll-hall-of-fame-nominees/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Rolling Stone</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/arts/music/story/2009/09/23/rock-hall-fame-nominees.html?ref=rss" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.billboard.com/news/kiss-genesis-chili-peppers-among-nominees-1004014961.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Billboard</i>)</a></li>
<li>The multi-billion dollar <a href="/wiki/King_Abdullah_University_of_Science_and_Technology" title="King Abdullah University of Science and Technology">King Abdullah University of Science and Technology</a>, boasting one of the world's fastest <a href="/wiki/Supercomputer" title="Supercomputer">supercomputers</a>, opens near <a href="/wiki/Jeddah" title="Jeddah">Jeddah</a> in <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> in an attempt to enable the country to compete in science and technology internationally. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8270601.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="President of the Czech Republic">President</a> <a href="/wiki/V%C3%A1clav_Klaus" title="Václav Klaus">Václav Klaus</a> says he is "adamant" <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Irish</a> voters will reject the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> when they vote on it again in the country's <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">2 October referendum</a>, meaning his unwillingness to sign the treaty will be justified. <a class="external text" href="http://aktualne.centrum.cz/czechnews/clanek.phtml?id=648356" rel="nofollow">(Aktualne)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libertas.eu" title="Libertas.eu">Libertas</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Declan_Ganley" title="Declan Ganley">Declan Ganley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ryanair" title="Ryanair">Ryanair</a> CEO <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_O%27Leary_(Ryanair)" title="Michael O'Leary (Ryanair)">Michael O'Leary</a> clash during high-profile radio and television debates on the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">referendum campaign</a> intensifies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/blogs/thereporters/gavinhewitt/2009/09/lisbon_fiercely_debated.html" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/national-news/oleary-and-ganley-lock-horns-in-bitter-tv-showdown-1896426.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_G-20_Pittsburgh_summit" title="2009 G-20 Pittsburgh summit">2009 G-20 Pittsburgh summit</a> commences with two dozen world leaders in attendance.</li>
<li>Sixteen members of <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">al-Qaeda</a>, five of whom have been sentenced to death, are at large after escaping from prison north of <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8272744.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Chandrayaan-1" title="Chandrayaan-1">Chandrayaan-1</a> probe discovers large amounts of water on the <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">Moon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/news/298416_Water-detected-on-moon-by-Chandrayaan--ISRO-says-path-breaking" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/607e2b60-a911-11de-b8bd-00144feabdc0.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/24/content_12107884.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,26121830-30417,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/science/2009/sep/24/discovery-water-moon-lunar-base" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">Security Council</a>, headed by world leaders, unanimously approve Resolution 1887 to prevent the proliferation of <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapon" title="Nuclear weapon">nuclear weapons</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8272396.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/world/2009-09/24/content_8733432.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/25/world/25prexy.html?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jgipm0XJZREav4IStxO6HzUn0nAwD9ATP44G0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hindustantimes.com/News/world/UNSC-adopts-N-resolution-asks-non-NPT-states-to-join-treaty/Article1-457658.aspx" rel="nofollow">(<i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> and the U.S. Army announce a breakthrough of a <a href="/wiki/HIV" title="HIV">HIV</a>/<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AIDS" title="AIDS">AIDS</a> vaccine, after trials find it can reduce infection by 31%. <a class="external text" href="http://enews.mcot.net/view.php?id=11979" rel="nofollow">(Thai News Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bernama.com/bernama/v5/newsindex.php?id=442189" rel="nofollow">(Bernama)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/24/content_12107259.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/worldservice/news/2009/09/090924_aids_vaccine_sl.shtml" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/HEALTH/09/24/hiv.vaccine/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur%27s_Day" title="Arthur's Day">Arthur's Day</a>: The 250th anniversary of the signing of a lease by <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Guinness" title="Arthur Guinness">Arthur Guinness</a> for <a href="/wiki/Guinness_Brewery" title="Guinness Brewery">a brewery at St James's Gate</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>. Events organised by <a href="/wiki/Diageo" title="Diageo">Diageo</a> get underway in Dublin, <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lagos" title="Lagos">Lagos</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yaound%C3%A9" title="Yaoundé">Yaoundé</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0924/guinness.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/ireland/2009/0924/1224255127163.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philly.com/inquirer/business/20090924_Guinness_celebrates_250th_birthday.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philadelphia Inquirer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Guinness-Celebrates-250th-Anniversary-Since-Founder-Signed-9000-Year-Lease-At-Brewery/Article/200909415387740?lpos=World_News_First_World_News_Feature_Teaser_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15387740_Guinness_Celebrates_250th_Anniversary_Since_Founder_Signed_9%2C000_Year_Lease_At_Brewery_" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>The last surviving <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ertu%C4%9Frul_Osman" title="Ertuğrul Osman">Ertuğrul Osman</a>, dies in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> at the age of 97. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8273396.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.todayszaman.com/tz-web/news-187867-101-osmanoglu-the-eldest-ottoman-dynasty-member-passes-away.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Today's Zaman</i>)</a></li>
<li>Nine <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Koreans</a> enter <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>'s embassy in the <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnamese</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Hanoi" title="Hanoi">Hanoi</a> to seek <a href="/wiki/Right_of_asylum" title="Right of asylum">political asylum</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8272482.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.etaiwannews.com/etn/news_content.php?id=1065304&amp;lang=eng_news" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taiwan News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/09/25/world/asia/25korea.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>An online petition is launched after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_The_Gambia" title="List of heads of state of The Gambia">President</a> of <a href="/wiki/The_Gambia" title="The Gambia">The Gambia</a> <a href="/wiki/Yahya_Jammeh" title="Yahya Jammeh">Yahya Jammeh</a> threatens to kill human rights workers that "destabilise" the country. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8272774.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.newstimeafrica.com/archives/2399" rel="nofollow">(Newstime Africa)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> begins clearing up after its <a href="/wiki/2009_Australian_dust_storm" title="2009 Australian dust storm">worst dust storm in seven decades</a>, which smothered <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a> and brought transport to a standstill. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8272128.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Staffordshire_hoard" title="Staffordshire hoard">largest haul</a> of <a href="/wiki/Anglo-Saxons" title="Anglo-Saxons">Anglo-Saxon</a> treasure, a collection of 1,500 gold and silver pieces comparable to the <a href="/wiki/Book_of_Kells" title="Book of Kells">Book of Kells</a>, is discovered buried beneath a field in <a href="/wiki/Staffordshire" title="Staffordshire">Staffordshire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/england/staffordshire/8272058.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/uk/2009/sep/24/anglo-saxon-treasure-hoard-gold-staffordshire-metal-detector" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/uk/article6847081.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/uknews/6225100/Britains-largest-Anglo-Saxon-gold-hoard.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/golden-dreams-for-man-with-the-golden-metal-detector-1792390.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0924/gold.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://story.malaysiasun.com/index.php/ct/9/cid/b8de8e630faf3631/id/546729/cs/1/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysian Sun</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,26119804-12377,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>The <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mail" title="Daily Mail">Daily Mail</a></i> newspapers apologise to <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a>, the manager of <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>'s <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">national football team</a>, after printing pictures of him and his wife Laura resting in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mud-bath" title="Mud-bath">mud-baths</a> on an <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> beach. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/8272510.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> agrees to develop 1,000 km<sup>2</sup> (386 sq miles) of farmland in <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090924084905703C603651" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8272506.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.koreaherald.co.kr/NEWKHSITE/data/html_dir/2009/09/24/200909240088.asp" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Korea Herald</i>)</a></li>
