<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Photographs of <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Spain" title="Prime Minister of Spain">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Rodr%C3%ADguez_Zapatero" title="José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero">José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero</a> and his family are published in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and subsequently published on the front pages of newspapers in his home country. A controversy occurs as many Spaniards have never before seen the children of the intensely private Prime Minister. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/25/spain-zapatero-daughters-obama" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> approves a law making <a href="/wiki/Chemical_castration" title="Chemical castration">chemical castration</a> mandatory for <a href="/wiki/Pedophilia" title="Pedophilia">paedophiles</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSTRE58O4LE20090925" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Four people are charged in <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> over recent bombing attacks, in the first arrests brought against suspected terrorists in several years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=3&amp;art_id=nw20090925135838586C554192" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5jhVC4thvCOZqGNWBW-u1cvrzepoA" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigerian</a> MPs ask the government to investigate the status of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> citizens living in the country, after allegations that Nigerians in China have been mistreated. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8274755.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The trial of former <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ehud_Olmert" title="Ehud Olmert">Ehud Olmert</a> on corruption charges begins in <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>. He is the first ever Israeli Prime Minister to be brought to trial. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/8274116.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0925/olmerte.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> reveals to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> nuclear watchdog the existence of a second <a href="/wiki/Enriched_uranium" title="Enriched uranium">uranium enrichment</a> plant, facing accusations of secret building projects from <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/in_depth/8274262.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/hasen/spages/1117043.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0925/iran.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>Lawyers for the former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister of France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dominique_de_Villepin" title="Dominique de Villepin">Dominique de Villepin</a>, say they will sue <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> for having called him "guilty" of the "<a href="/wiki/Clearstream" title="Clearstream">Clearstream</a>" affair and violating the principle of <a href="/wiki/Presumption_of_innocence" title="Presumption of innocence">presumption of innocence</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8274314.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>At least two people are killed and fifteen injured in a blast at a fireworks shop in <a href="/wiki/Santo_Andr%C3%A9,_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Santo André, São Paulo">Santo André</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greater_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Greater São Paulo">Greater São Paulo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8273911.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/25/content_12110373.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/crime/20090925/156245950.html" rel="nofollow">(Ria Novosti)</a></li>
<li>Hundreds of people queue in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham" title="Birmingham">Birmingham</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, to see part of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Staffordshire_hoard" title="Staffordshire hoard">Staffordshire hoard</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/england/staffordshire/8274279.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a> is to create the world's first "<a href="/wiki/Shark" title="Shark">shark</a> sanctuary", banning all <a href="/wiki/Commercial_fishing" title="Commercial fishing">commercial shark fishing</a> in its waters. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/science/nature/8272508.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/environment/article6848627.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Science_News/2009/09/25/Palau-to-create-shark-sanctuary/UPI-25501253888487/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paul_G._Kirk,_Jr." title="Paul G. Kirk, Jr.">Paul G. Kirk, Jr.</a> is sworn in as the <a href="/wiki/Interim" title="Interim">interim</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Senator" title="U.S. Senator">U.S. Senator</a> from <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a>, succeeding the late <a href="/wiki/Ted_Kennedy" title="Ted Kennedy">Ted Kennedy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rollcall.com/news/38951-1.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Roll Call</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Second <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=South_America-Africa_Summit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="South America-Africa Summit (page does not exist)">South America-Africa Summit</a> (ASA) on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Isla_Margarita" title="Isla Margarita">Isla Margarita</a>:
<ul>
<li>The second <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=South_America-Africa_Summit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="South America-Africa Summit (page does not exist)">South America-Africa Summit</a> (ASA) begins on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Isla_Margarita" title="Isla Margarita">Isla Margarita</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12114739.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601086&amp;sid=as7b1b_qZApE" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/BT-CO-20090925-712414.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li>30 African and South American leaders arrive to attend, with 60 countries being represented. <a class="external text" href="http://english.cctv.com/program/newshour/20090927/103103.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CCTV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=68&amp;art_id=nw20090927102243343C656909" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South African</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Africa" title="President of South Africa">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Zuma" title="Jacob Zuma">Jacob Zuma</a> says during the opening of the summit that the South-South union between South American and African regions will contribute to the development of both. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12114951.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> says regional governments are to sign an agreement to create a Bank of the South with startup capital of 20 billion US dollars. <a class="external text" href="http://www.walesonline.co.uk/news/latest-world-news/2009/09/27/seven-nations-to-fund-regional-bank-claims-chavez-91466-24791294/" rel="nofollow">(Wales Online)</a></li>
<li>A regional bank for <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">Bank of the South</a>, with a $20-billion initial capital is then set up under an agreement signed by seven nations—<a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>—on the sidelines of the summit. <a class="external text" href="http://www.apanews.net/apa.php?page=show_article_eng&amp;id_article=107668" rel="nofollow">(African Press Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2009/09/27/south-american-leaders-sign-agreement-creating-south-bank" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> calls for the creation of a military alliance among nations in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Atlantic" title="South Atlantic">South Atlantic</a> region by 2011, calling it "NATO of the South". <a class="external text" href="http://www.rttnews.com/Content/GeneralNews.aspx?Node=B1&amp;Id=1077523" rel="nofollow">(RTTNews)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>More than 100 ministers and heads of state attend a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> meeting on the global hunger crisis. <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Bangladesh" title="Prime Minister of Bangladesh">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Hasina" title="Sheikh Hasina">Sheikh Hasina</a> tables a five-pronged set of recommendations to raise a hunger-free world. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12115738.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0927/powerp.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://bdnews24.com/details.php?id=143572&amp;cid=2" rel="nofollow">(Bangldesh News)</a></li>
<li>At least 10 people are dead in <a href="/wiki/Metro_Manila" title="Metro Manila">Metro Manila</a> after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Ketsana_(2009)" title="Tropical Storm Ketsana (2009)">Tropical Storm Ketsana</a> hits the northern <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iRUDyeGrHCZ6Bd9LyEdrne0FN6hA" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/nation/view/20090926-227047/Floods-submerge-Metro-Manila-areas" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippines Inquirer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8276347.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/Article.aspx?articleId=508807&amp;publicationSubCategoryId=63" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Star</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Guantanamo_Bay_detainees" title="List of Guantanamo Bay detainees">Three detainees held</a> by the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> at <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_Naval_Base" title="Guantanamo Bay Naval Base">Guantánamo Bay</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, are sent abroad to two countries. <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> accepts two detainees of <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbeki</a> origin in a humanitarian gesture, with <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Justice_and_Equality" title="Minister for Justice and Equality">Minister for Justice, Equality and Law Reform</a> <a href="/wiki/Dermot_Ahern" title="Dermot Ahern">Dermot Ahern</a> saying Ireland was one of the first countries in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> to call for the closure of Guantánamo Bay and that the two men would now be given time to rebuild their lives. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE58P28P20090926" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2009/0927/guantanamo.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/8277140.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenyan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Kenya" title="List of heads of state of Kenya">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mwai_Kibaki" title="Mwai Kibaki">Mwai Kibaki</a> writes to <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> to express his concern and disappointment over threats it has received from that country concerning a travel ban on Kenyan officials it blames for hindering reforms. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=87&amp;art_id=nw20090926172618406C728364" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> blasts kill at least 12 people in northwestern <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/featuredCrisis/idUSSP396592" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2009/09/200992625241814252.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/pakistan/14-killed-in-renewed-suicide-attacks-in-Pakistans-NWFP/articleshow/5058770.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>

<li>Families separated for over 50 years since the <a href="/wiki/Korean_War" title="Korean War">Korean War</a> meet at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/K%C5%ADmgangsan_Tourist_Region" title="Kŭmgangsan Tourist Region">Kŭmgangsan resort</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8276063.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/northkorea/2009/09/26/38/0401000000AEN20090926002600315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jTg7x7snBEMQtr6aJWU_5ZAPbwkgD9AUV7V00" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/26/content_12114092.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> announces it is to establish <a href="/wiki/Armenia%E2%80%93Turkey_relations" title="Armenia–Turkey relations">formal diplomatic relations</a> with <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a> on October 10. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hurriyetdailynews.com/n.php?n=turkey-armenia-to-sign-diplomatic-deal-next-month-says-official-2009-09-27" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hurriyet</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/europe/8277835.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a> denies rumours concerning his health as the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">Labour Party</a> gathers for its conference in <a href="/wiki/Brighton" title="Brighton">Brighton</a>, expressing his amazement with <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Marr" title="Andrew Marr">Andrew Marr</a> of the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> for questioning him live on television. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/politics/article6851283.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/newstopics/politics/gordon-brown/6237419/BBC-stuns-Gordon-Brown-with-question-on-pill-taking.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> the <a href="/wiki/CDU/CSU" title="CDU/CSU">Christian Democrats</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Free_Democratic_Party_of_Germany" title="Free Democratic Party of Germany">Liberals</a> win the <a href="/wiki/German_federal_election,_2009" title="German federal election, 2009">federal election</a> and announce their intention to form a new government with <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> as <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">Chancellor</a>. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SPD" title="SPD">Social Democrats</a> concede defeat. <a class="external text" href="http://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/0,1518,651610,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Der Spiegel</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/germany/6237210/Merkels-rival-concedes-defeat-in-German-election.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net//news/europe/2009/09/200992716816398639.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Party_(Portugal)" title="Socialist Party (Portugal)">Socialist Party</a> win the <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portuguese</a> <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_legislative_election,_2009" title="Portuguese legislative election, 2009">legislative election</a> to elect members of the <a href="/wiki/Assembly_of_the_Republic_(Portugal)" title="Assembly of the Republic (Portugal)">Assembly of the Republic</a>, with 36.6% of the vote. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2009/09/28/portuguese-elections-results/" rel="nofollow">(euronews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/portugal-keeps-socialists-in-power-despite-slump-1794269.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.trend.az/regions/world/europe/1548038.html" rel="nofollow">(Trend News Agency)</a></li>
<li>Second <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=South_America-Africa_Summit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="South America-Africa Summit (page does not exist)">South America-Africa Summit</a> (ASA) on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Isla_Margarita" title="Isla Margarita">Isla Margarita</a>:
<ul>
<li>The leaders of <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a>, call on the continents of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a> to unite to secure prosperity for future generations. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2009/09/20099271133771129.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE58Q00A20090927" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8277016.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> says that ASA member countries have achieved concrete results since the 1st ASA Summit in <a href="/wiki/Abuja" title="Abuja">Abuja</a> in 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12116296.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Film director <a href="/wiki/Roman_Polanski" title="Roman Polanski">Roman Polanski</a> is arrested in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zurich" title="Zurich">Zurich</a> on a 31-year-old US arrest warrant. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/entertainment/8277176.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.portalangop.co.ao/motix/en_us/noticias/internacional/2009/8/39/Roman-Polanski-held-Zurich,81730528-edaa-4033-8393-f39d6f6825d8.html" rel="nofollow">(Angola Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> Energy Minister <a href="/wiki/Ismail_Khan" title="Ismail Khan">Ismail Khan</a> survives a roadside blast which kills four people and wounds seventeen outside a school in <a href="/wiki/Herat" title="Herat">Herat</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/8277048.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/south-asia/Afghan-energy-minister-survives-roadside-attack-four-civilians-killed/articleshow/5061909.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Ketsana_(2009)" title="Tropical Storm Ketsana (2009)">Tropical Storm Ketsana</a> rises to 73, with more than 300,000 people displaced. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/nation/view/20090927-227130/73-dead-more-than-300000-displaced-by-Ondoy" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Inquirer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8277018.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/world/2009-09/27/content_8743411.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>China Daily</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Swiss</a> multinational <a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestlé">Nestlé</a> is buying milk from a farm seized from its white owners and now owned by the wife of <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Zimbabwe" title="List of Presidents of Zimbabwe">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a>, according to <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Telegraph" title="The Sunday Telegraph">The Sunday Telegraph</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8277481.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> <a href="/wiki/General_(United_States)" title="General (United States)">General</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stanley_McChrystal" title="Stanley McChrystal">Stanley McChrystal</a>, Commander of the <a href="/wiki/International_Security_Assistance_Force" title="International Security Assistance Force">International Security Assistance Force</a>, formally requests more troops for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001-present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001-present)">War in Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/8276996.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> television series <i><a href="/wiki/Family_Guy" title="Family Guy">Family Guy</a></i> is outlawed by authorities in <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> due to <a href="/wiki/420_(Family_Guy)" title="420 (Family Guy)">an episode</a> promoting the <a href="/wiki/Legality_of_cannabis" title="Legality of cannabis">legalization</a> and use of <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_(drug)" title="Cannabis (drug)">marijuana</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8277129.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Army_of_the_Guardians_of_the_Islamic_Revolution" title="Army of the Guardians of the Islamic Revolution">Revolutionary Guards</a> test fire several short-range missiles – the <a href="/wiki/Fateh-110" title="Fateh-110">Fateh-110</a> and Tondar-69. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail.aspx?id=107220&amp;sectionid=351020101" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.chosun.com/site/data/html_dir/2009/09/27/2009092700639.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chosun Ilbo</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/iranian-military-stages-missile-exercises-1794069.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12117776.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Premier</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> tells a rally in <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a> about his encounters with <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, saying: "What's his name? Some tanned guy... Ah, Barack Obama!", also commenting on his wife <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Obama" title="Michelle Obama">Michelle</a>: "You won't believe it, but two of them went to the beach because the wife is also tanned". <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=3&amp;art_id=nw20090927223141133C260445" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/italy/6237409/Silvio-Berlusconi-calls-Barack-Obama-tanned---again.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> issues a 10-day deadline to <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> asking it to decide the status of deposed <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a>, who is residing in its embassy in the capital <a href="/wiki/Tegucigalpa" title="Tegucigalpa">Tegucigalpa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/americas/09/27/honduras.presidemt/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSTRE58Q0A320090927" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Discworld" title="Discworld">Discworld</a></i> author <a href="/wiki/Terry_Pratchett" title="Terry Pratchett">Terry Pratchett</a>, who has <a href="/wiki/Alzheimer%27s_disease" title="Alzheimer's disease">Alzheimer's disease</a>, criticises new guidelines on <a href="/wiki/Assisted_suicide" title="Assisted suicide">assisted suicide</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/england/bristol/somerset/8277228.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An award-winning essay written by <a href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney" title="Paul McCartney">Paul McCartney</a> as a 10-year-old for the <a href="/wiki/Coronation_of_the_British_monarch" title="Coronation of the British monarch">coronation</a> of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Elizabeth II of the United Kingdom">Elizabeth II of the United Kingdom</a> is found after lying undiscovered in <a href="/wiki/Liverpool" title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Central_Library" title="Liverpool Central Library">Central Library</a> for more than 50 years. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/8277008.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/music/2009/sep/27/paul-mccartney-schoolboy-essay-found" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/arts/music/story/2009/09/27/mccartney-essay-library.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nme.com/news/paul-mccartney/47532" rel="nofollow">(<i>NME</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://entertainment.timesonline.co.uk/tol/arts_and_entertainment/music/beatles/article6850826.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sunday Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Four people injured in a <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South African</a> plane crash in <a href="/wiki/Durban" title="Durban">Durban</a> on Thursday are still recovering in hospital. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=13&amp;art_id=nw20090927222505597C235319" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 28, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-28</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_28&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_28&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> students at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Tehran" title="University of Tehran">University of Tehran</a> demonstrate against the government on the first day of the new academic year. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/8279193.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thelede.blogs.nytimes.com/2009/09/28/students-protest-at-tehran-university/?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/internetNews/idINTRE58R4DS20090928" rel="nofollow">(Reuters India)</a></li>
<li>Opponents of the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> question the <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> on deliberate interference in the <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">Irish referendum campaign</a> in order to secure its desired "Yes" vote, suggesting that the Commission has broken the law. <a class="external text" href="http://euobserver.com/9/28730" rel="nofollow">(<i>EU Observer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2009/0928/breaking74.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muammar_al-Gaddafi" title="Muammar al-Gaddafi">Muammar al-Gaddafi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> sign eight accords in <a href="/wiki/Caracas" title="Caracas">Caracas</a> following the weekend's second ASA summit. <a class="external text" href="http://www.laht.com/article.asp?ArticleId=344500&amp;CategoryId=10717" rel="nofollow">(<i>Latin American Herald Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/27/content_12115907.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>The death toll in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Ketsana_(2009)" title="Typhoon Ketsana (2009)">worst flooding</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> for forty years reaches 140 as the capital <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a> is "overwhelmed". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/28/philippines-storm-death-toll" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/world/asia/article6852358.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/asia/philippines/6239022/Philippine-flood-death-toll-rises.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roman_Polanski" title="Roman Polanski">Roman Polanski</a> officially challenges his proposed <a href="/wiki/Extradition" title="Extradition">extradition</a> from <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> to face <a href="/wiki/Child_sexual_abuse" title="Child sexual abuse">child sexual abuse</a> charges stemming from a 1977 incident. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/ap/20090929/ap_on_en_mo/eu_switzerland_polanski" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">Liberal Democratic Party</a> elects <a href="/wiki/Sadakazu_Tanigaki" title="Sadakazu Tanigaki">Sadakazu Tanigaki</a> to replace <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taro_Aso" title="Taro Aso">Taro Aso</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8278567.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.etaiwannews.com/etn/news_content.php?id=1068372&amp;lang=eng_news" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taiwan News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/28/content_12122974.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Those in power in <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> empower police to quash "unauthorised" gatherings as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a> calls on his supporters to march on the three-month anniversary of his fall, saying it will be "the final offensive". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/28/honduras-suspends-civil-liberties-zelaya" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Eldoret" title="Eldoret">Eldoret</a> operation commences to close down <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>'s largest camp for people forced to flee their homes during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%932008_Kenyan_crisis" title="2007–2008 Kenyan crisis">2007–2008 Kenyan crisis</a> ethnic violence. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8278051.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Politics_of_Southern_Sudan" title="Politics of Southern Sudan">President of the autonomous Government of Southern Sudan</a> <a href="/wiki/Salva_Kiir_Mayardit" title="Salva Kiir Mayardit">Salva Kiir</a> says <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> is at a "historic crossroads" which will lead to a split from the north. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8278130.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/Africa/2009-09-28-voa4.cfm" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/The_Twelve_Apostles_(Victoria)" title="The Twelve Apostles (Victoria)">12 Apostles</a> natural landmarks continue to crumble. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/travel/news/article6851240.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Little_Cumbrae" title="Little Cumbrae">Little Cumbrae</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a> is converted into an <a href="/wiki/Ashram" title="Ashram">ashram</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/scotland/glasgow_and_west/8277970.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Charges of plotting to topple <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a> against <a href="/wiki/Jestina_Mukoko" title="Jestina Mukoko">Jestina Mukoko</a>, a prominent <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwean</a> rights activist, are thrown out after the Supreme Court rules she had been tortured while in custody. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8278178.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/reuters/2009/09/28/world/international-us-zimbabwe-rights.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gr%C3%A9goire_Ndahimana" title="Grégoire Ndahimana">Grégoire Ndahimana</a>, a former mayor accused of taking part in the 1994 <a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwandan</a> genocide, pleads not guilty at a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> tribunal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/feedarticle/8728061" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8278435.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.theage.com.au/breaking-news-world/mayor-faces-court-over-rwanda-massacre-20090928-g92a.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Age</i>)</a></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Chinese_Civilisation_Revisited&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Chinese Civilisation Revisited (page does not exist)">Chinese Civilisation Revisited</a></i> by Xiao Jiansheng, a book about <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> history which is outlawed in China, goes on sale in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8278014.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.asiaone.com/News/Latest%2BNews/Asia/Story/A1Story20090928-170503.html" rel="nofollow">(AsiaOne)</a></li>
<li>A police officer who served at the <a href="/wiki/G20" title="G20">G20</a> demonstrations in London in April 2009 is to face a charge of assaulting a woman with a baton after becoming involved in a confrontation at a vigil for <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Ian_Tomlinson" title="Death of Ian Tomlinson">Ian Tomlinson</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/uk/crime/article6852445.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/finance/financetopics/g20-summit/6239763/Police-sergeant-who-struck-G20-protestor-faces-assault-charge.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Pablo_Pineda" title="Pablo Pineda">Pablo Pineda</a> wins the best actor award at the <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_International_Film_Festival" title="San Sebastián International Film Festival">San Sebastián International Film Festival</a>, the first actor with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Down%27s_syndrome" title="Down's syndrome">Down's syndrome</a> to win an international film award. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/entertainment/8278108.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thinkspain.com/news-spain/17116/downs-syndrome-actor-wins-award-at-san-sebastian-film-festival" rel="nofollow">(Think Spain)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.laht.com/article.asp?ArticleId=344501&amp;CategoryId=13003" rel="nofollow">(<i>Latin American Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li>Art historian Henry Adams claims <a href="/wiki/Abstract_expressionism" title="Abstract expressionism">abstract impressionist</a> <a href="/wiki/Jackson_Pollock" title="Jackson Pollock">Jackson Pollock</a> camouflaged his signature as a "hidden message" inside his famous 1943 <i>Mural</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/art/art-news/6238696/Jackson-Pollock-hid-signature-inside-88m-painting.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> revises its <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_North_Korea" title="Constitution of North Korea">constitution</a>, removing all references to <a href="/wiki/Communism" title="Communism">communism</a>, while mentioning <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> for the first time, as well as stating <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a> as its "Supreme Leader". <a class="external text" href="http://www.rthk.org.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/news.htm?main&amp;20090929&amp;56&amp;615725" rel="nofollow">(RTHK)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hY5_VJJzvCxgWdthfrbI1iDU4CsQD9B0A13O0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.koreatimes.co.kr/www/news/nation/2009/09/116_52641.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Korea Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/latestCrisis/idUSSEO253213" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>At least 58 people are killed at a large <a href="/wiki/2009_Guinea_protest" title="2009 Guinea protest">opposition rally</a> in <a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinea</a> against <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Dadis_Camara" title="Moussa Dadis Camara">Moussa Dadis Camara</a> who seized power in a coup last year. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8279103.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/29/content_12123247.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/200992815223645889.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The interim government in <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> raids two media outlets critical of the government, and suspends other <a href="/wiki/Civil_liberties" title="Civil liberties">civil liberties</a> for 45 days. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/americas/8279243.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jAkMGKIUDg_ngUiZboxQbYj5_DPwD9B0D6P80" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2009/09/2009928124228951255.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Oxfam" title="Oxfam">Oxfam</a> launches an emergency appeal for £9.5 million for <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> and other <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">East African</a> countries to fight the worst drought in a decade. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/8279796.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peruvian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Peru" title="List of Presidents of Peru">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Alberto_Fujimori" title="Alberto Fujimori">Alberto Fujimori</a> pleads guilty to bribery and illegal phone-tapping of journalists, businessmen and opposition politicians. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8279528.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>At least 40 people are killed as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Ketsana_(2009)" title="Typhoon Ketsana (2009)">Typhoon Ketsana</a> makes landfall on <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/news/306116_Typhoon-Ketsana-kills-31-in-Vietnam--officials" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2009-09/29/content_12131817.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> upholds a <a href="/wiki/Flagellation" title="Flagellation">whipping</a> punishment for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kartika_Sari_Dewi_Shukarno" title="Kartika Sari Dewi Shukarno">Kartika Sari Dewi Shukarno</a> who was convicted of drinking <a href="/wiki/Beer" title="Beer">beer</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2009/9/29/courts/4801563&amp;sec=courts" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Star</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2009/09/2009929524586283.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">President of Peru</a> <a href="/wiki/Alberto_Fujimori" title="Alberto Fujimori">Alberto Fujimori</a> pleads guilty to charges of <a href="/wiki/Bribery" title="Bribery">bribery</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spying" title="Spying">spying</a> on his old rivals during his presidency. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/world/view/20090929-227447/Perus-Fujimori-admits-to-corruption-charges" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> denies accusations that it broke <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>'s laws against using taxpayers' money on <a href="/wiki/Referendum" title="Referendum">referendum</a> spending after an EU office in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a> paid €150,000 to insert a guide to the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a> into all Sunday newspapers as the <a href="/wiki/Twenty-eighth_Amendment_of_the_Constitution_of_Ireland" title="Twenty-eighth Amendment of the Constitution of Ireland">country's second referendum</a> approaches. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/ireland/2009/0929/1224255442147.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Member_of_the_European_Parliament" title="Member of the European Parliament">MEP</a> <a href="/wiki/Patricia_McKenna" title="Patricia McKenna">Patricia McKenna</a> promises legal action against any newspapers found carrying the Commission's guide, with legal advisers to Europe's <a href="/wiki/Council_of_the_European_Union" title="Council of the European Union">Council of Ministers</a> expressing "some concern" about its content. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/ireland/2009/0929/1224255442147.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least 87 people die in a crackdown by the <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Guinea" title="Military of Guinea">Military of Guinea</a> on an opposition rally against the country's leader <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Dadis_Camara" title="Moussa Dadis Camara">Moussa Dadis Camara</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8280603.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/200992981337765437.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a>'s constitutional court recounts votes from last month's <a href="/wiki/Gabonese_presidential_election,_2009" title="Gabonese presidential election, 2009">disputed presidential election</a> won by the son of longtime leader <a href="/wiki/Omar_Bongo" title="Omar Bongo">Omar Bongo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.int.iol.co.za/index.php?set_id=1&amp;click_id=86&amp;art_id=nw20090927102128474C687471" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a></li>
<li>A 14-year-old schoolgirl in <a href="/wiki/Coventry" title="Coventry">Coventry</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, who died after being given a <a href="/wiki/Cervical_cancer" title="Cervical cancer">cervical cancer</a> vaccine as part of that country's national immunisation programme is found to have suffered from a tumor in her heart and lungs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/life_and_style/health/article6852858.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/health/8279656.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/33117752/ns/health-cancer/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>An 8.3 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">magnitude</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Samoa_earthquake" title="2009 Samoa earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Samoa_Islands" title="Samoa Islands">Samoa Islands</a>, triggering a <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunami</a> that kills at least 20 in the nation of <a href="/wiki/Samoa" title="Samoa">Samoa</a> and another 14 in <a href="/wiki/American_Samoa" title="American Samoa">American Samoa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSN2916050620090929" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/8281616.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 30, 2009<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2009-09-30</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_30&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_30&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2009_September_30&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The death toll from an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Samoa_earthquake" title="2009 Samoa earthquake">earthquake</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunami</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Samoan_Islands" title="Samoan Islands">Samoan Islands</a> region in the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">South Pacific</a> rises to at least 113. <a class="external text" href="http://news.theage.com.au/breaking-news-world/at-least-113-dead-in-pacific-tsunami-officials-20090930-gbzj.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Age</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5j9ul6SX_wYtgQi-cm_S5aA8et18Q" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li>A 7.6 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">magnitude</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009_Padang_earthquake" title="2009 Padang earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes western <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, killing at least 75 and trapping thousands of people under rubble. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE58T39720090930" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2009/sep/30/indonesia-earthquake-padang" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thejakartaglobe.com/home/thousands-trapped-under-rubble-in-indonesia-after-sumatra-earthquake-official/332769" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Globe</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinea</a>'s military leader Captain <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Dadis_Camara" title="Moussa Dadis Camara">Moussa Dadis Camara</a> bans all "subversive" gatherings and demonstrations in the aftermath of <a href="/wiki/2009_Guinea_protest" title="2009 Guinea protest">opposition protests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/8282186.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5iAVjutFiNxMjNLZd6fFZMANVHAXgD9B1JG0O0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a></li>
<li>Diplomatic officials from the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a> hold their first high level meetings in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/news/306465_US-Burma-dialogue-begin--monks-demand-timeline" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/8281970.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>24 people are killed and 62 injured after a <a href="/wiki/Church_(building)" title="Church (building)">church</a> collapses in <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news/world/south-asia/Church-collapse-in-Nepal-kills-24/articleshow/5070789.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hVzNffNsc2FaZlJ1u8kqGkM09dUgD9B1DLPG0" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehimalayantimes.com/fullNews.php?headline=Church+collapse+kills+23+in+Dharan&amp;NewsID=36045" rel="nofollow">(<i>Himalayan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Ketsana_(2009)" title="Typhoon Ketsana (2009)">Typhoon Ketsana</a> across <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a> rises to 300. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5i6eatUwlDQQIHZiKqXjLHTmQSrogD9B1HABO2" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2009/WORLD/asiapcf/09/30/vietnam.typhoon.ketsana.toll/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> is to <a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">withdraw</a> 4,000 troops from <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> by the end of October. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2009/09/20099307597965129.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2009/09/29/AR2009092904133.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Several <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> political parties boycott a conference on the future of <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2009/09/200992992348587440.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The final report of an <a href="/wiki/Heidi_Tagliavini#EU_fact-finding_mission" title="Heidi Tagliavini">international fact-finding mission</a> concludes that <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> started the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/2009/09/30/world/AP-EU-Russia-Georgia.html?_r=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Peru" title="List of Presidents of Peru">President</a> of <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a> <a href="/wiki/Alberto_Fujimori" title="Alberto Fujimori">Alberto Fujimori</a> is sentenced to six years in jail for corruption by a court in <a href="/wiki/Lima" title="Lima">Lima</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/8283844.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Worldwide"><a href="/wiki/World" title="World">Worldwide</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/September_2009/Sidebar&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-6" title="Portal:Current events/September 2009/Sidebar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul>
